German Representative Sharply Refutes French Remarks 64

Denies Police are a Disguised Army

Geneva, 16th (National News Agency) - German representative Rosenberg, in a conversation with journalists, vehemently refuted French representative Massigli's statement that the German police could be regarded as an armed force. He stated that out of the 140,000 police in Germany, 35,000 are city police, responsible for managing street traffic and minor matters; 18,000 are engaged in clerical work; and the remaining 87,000 are under the jurisdiction of the 17 states, not managed by the federal government. Furthermore, the German police do not possess any powerful weapons such as field artillery, and the number of machine guns is regulated by the Allied Control Commission. Even armored vehicles are merely automobiles protected by steel plates, far from comparable to military armored vehicles. To claim that these police have military value is simply laughable. He also stated that the occasional exercises resembling military maneuvers by the police are solely for the purpose of preparing for riot prevention. Finally, he emphasized that comparing this matter to the issue of hundreds of thousands of troops and millions of dollars worth of military equipment is trivial.

Geneva, 15th (Havas) - The chief German delegate to the League of Nations Assembly, Rosenberg, addressed the international press, refuting the French delegate Massigli's explanation of the German police yesterday. Rosenberg's main rebuttals were as follows: (1) The German police organization is not uniform, nor is there a unified command. The national police are divided among 17 states and are unrelated to the federal government. (2) The organization and armament of the German police were determined after several consultations with the Ambassador's Conference and the military supervision committees of the League of Nations countries. This arrangement is precisely to prevent the police from being used in warfare. (3) The rules regarding the police are not secret. These rules show that the purpose of police training is indeed for police duties. (4) The demilitarized zone accounts for about one-sixth of the country's territory. Within this zone, the police are the only force maintaining order. It must be explained that at yesterday's meeting of the Military Affairs Committee, the chairman first stated that the committee's discussion involved this matter, so the French representative had to make a statement. Moreover, the discussion of President Hoover's proposal would happen sooner or later, and the French representative could not control it.

Issue of Location for the Four-Power Conference 65

France proposes holding it within the League of Nations framework, which Germany considers an intentional insult.

The British government is still working to mediate.

London, 15th (Reuters) - Following meetings between British Prime Minister MacDonald and French Prime Minister Herriot, the British government is still actively in contact with the German government regarding the Four-Power Conference. Sources in London with quick access to information are now hopeful that Germany's opposition to holding the meeting in Geneva will not be prolonged. The Hague or Lausanne are both acceptable options for holding the conference. The British government believes that the location of the meeting is not of great importance. What Britain wants is for the representatives of Britain, France, Germany, and Italy to meet informally in one place to find a way to continue the work of the disarmament conference, which has been stalled due to Germany's demands for military equipment. The tension between France and Germany seems to be increasing daily. Parisian newspapers criticize Germany's unwillingness to participate in the Four-Power Conference held in Geneva, calling it new evidence of Germany's desire to restore its military strength. German officials, on the other hand, point to the invitation to participate in the Geneva conference as an act of humiliation. They are particularly indignant about the French representative Massigli's statement in Geneva yesterday that the German police are part of the army. At the same time, the statement by semi-official Parisian sources that the Disarmament Conference must proceed, but whether the regulations it adopts should apply to Germany may be left for future determination, is also displeasing to the Germans. German officials believe that France wants Germany to participate in the Disarmament Conference, but is vaguely unaware of whether the decision-making methods can be applied to Germany.

Berlin, 15th (National News Agency) - According to reports from Paris, France has recently shown a willingness to compromise on the location of the meeting, saying that if Germany allows France's allies, such as Belgium, Poland, and Czechoslovakia, to also be invited to join the meeting, then France can recognize Lausanne as the location of the meeting. However, Berlin still considers this inappropriate. If France must invite its allies, then it seems that non-allied countries should also be considered for invitation so that Germany can participate sincerely.

Japan Decides to Greatly Increase Troops in Northeast 70

Infantry, artillery, and cavalry have been transferred to Shenyang in batches.

Organizing a large-scale international aviation company.

Reorganizing the Northeast Arsenal and greatly expanding it.

Beijing Correspondence: The Japanese side, seeing the futility of the appeasement policy towards the people of the Northeast and the armed resolution of small anti-Japanese organizations in recent years, has decided to change all previous plans and thoroughly eliminate the volunteer armies in various parts of the Northeast. Moreover, the situation in the Northeast has become even more tense due to the armed confrontation between Su Bingwen and Tang Juwu with the Japanese, which has actually accelerated the Japanese side's determination to implement this plan. The news obtained from various sources is compiled and recorded as follows: (1) In order to replenish the casualties and vacancies in the current troops stationed in the Northeast, and to increase their strength, the Japanese military has specially transferred some infantry, artillery, and cavalry from the home country in batches. More than 1,000 people from their original stationed troops have all been sent to the border of Rehe. Soon, the Japanese military will definitely take major actions in Rehe. The so-called armed immigrants are just a smokescreen for the international community. (2) In order to counteract China's opening of a new Euro-Asian air route, facilitate the external airmail of the puppet state, and make it easier to mobilize the home country's air force to bomb volunteer armies, the Japanese side will fund the organization of the "Manchukuo" International Aviation Corporation, sign a contract with the puppet government to give it de facto convenience. Along the South Manchurian Railway and various parts of the Northeast, in addition to all existing airfields, 250 extremely well-equipped aviation stations will be established. All sound detectors and anti-aircraft artillery teams will be attached to them. In order to actively realize this plan, personnel from the Osaka Aviation School, the Army Survey Bureau, and the Aviation Department of Mitsubishi Corporation have been sent to Manchuria to be responsible for carrying out the first batch of 30 pilots and 50 aircraft, which have recently been transported to Shenyang. (3) In order to facilitate the resolution of the armed anti-Japanese civilians in the Northeast, the Japanese side has decided to send personnel to reorganize the former Northeast Arsenal and divide it into five major parts: (A) Department for manufacturing aircraft, including the manufacture of other aircraft and their parts; (B) Department for manufacturing poison gas and other chemical warfare drugs and their raw materials. All the machinery required by this department will be transported from the Japanese poison gas manufacturing plant in Dalian to Shenyang for refitting. The location of its poison gas storage庫, to be set up in Shenyang or Dalian, is yet to be determined; (C) Department for manufacturing and repairing artillery pieces, including an anti-aircraft artillery factory; (D) Department for manufacturing bullets, which will also be responsible for manufacturing the most violent and brutal gas machine gun bullets; (E) Department for manufacturing gunpowder. In addition to these five major factories, if necessary in the future, a radio machinery factory will be established. Taking a comprehensive view of the above-mentioned articles, the Japanese plan is not only to eliminate the Northeast Volunteer Army, but also to plot to occupy Rehe and Mongolia, threaten North China, or even cause a second World War.

Now, the various government troops are preparing to encircle the bandits and annihilate them in one fell swoop. Rong Jingfang's division also launched an attack from Yanglinqiao, which belongs to Tongcheng County, and occupied Daban Town, a vital passage on the border of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi. Currently, Guo's division is in Yanxia, Longgang, and Hengshitan, Zhang Gang is in Yangxin and Daye, and Xie Bin is in Huangsha and Daban, each responsible for clearing the countryside. He Chengjun recently went to Longgang to inspect and then returned to Hankou. Fifth Division Recovers Hengfeng County Seat 72

Hengfeng is also a bandit's nest.

Remnants of bandits flee north across the Xin River.

Nanchang Correspondence: Hengfeng is located in eastern Jiangxi, between Dexing, Shangrao, Qianshan, and Yiyang. The terrain is complex and transportation is difficult. In 1928, it was occupied by Fang Zhimin's bandits. Although it has been recovered several times since then, the bandit influence is so deep that it is repeatedly lost. Two years ago, Fang Bandit took Hengfeng as the center of the two old Guangxin prefectures in the Chihua Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian and Anhui border and the Xin River basin. The pseudo-Jiangxi Northeast Revolutionary Committee, the pseudo-Jiangxi-Minbian Provincial Government, the Red Army School, the pseudo-Postal Bureau, the Agricultural and Industrial Bank, etc. were all set up in the county seat. The pseudo-arsenal and rear hospital were set up in Geyuan, which belongs to the county, which is an important bandit's nest. Last month, when Zhu Mao invaded the north, the Fifth Division of the National Army rushed to Fuzhou from Guixi. The troops south of eastern Jiangxi were thin. Fang and Shao bandits invaded the south from the north bank of the Xin River and invaded northern Fujian and eastern Zhejiang from Guangfeng, Shangrao, and Qianshan. Afterwards, Chong'an and Pucheng were recovered by officials and generals in Fujian and Zhejiang. The bandit pseudo-Tenth Army fled to the border of Fujian and Zhejiang. At that time, the Fifth Division returned to Guixi from Fuzhou, and went east from Yiyang, and made a fierce advance to Hengfeng. At the same time, Zhao Guantao's troops were in the upper reaches of the Xin River in Shangrao and Guangfeng, Li Yunheng's division was on the north bank of the Xin River in Wannian and Leping, and Wang Jin's division was on the south bank of the Xin River in Qianshan He Kou, and encircled the bandits on a large scale. Fulin in Wannian, Zhoufang in Guixi, and Chepan in Qianshan were all important bandit nests that Fang bandits had occupied for many years, and they were successively recovered by the Li and Wang divisions. Hengfeng was the only county that Fang bandits relied on to resist stubbornly. Therefore, Hengfeng was also the last stronghold of the Red Bandits in northeastern Jiangxi. According to military news, Zhou Hunyuan, the commander of the Fifth Division, pursued Fang Shao from Guixi and advanced to Yiyang. At that time, a fierce battle occurred with the bandits. Zhou's division fought bravely and defeated the bandits. The two regiments of Zhou Jianping's 83rd and 84th of the pseudo-Tenth Army were completely disarmed by the government army, and the remaining remnants fled north across the Xin River in a mess. They are being pursued. According to news from the provincial government, Zhou Hunyuan, the commander of the Fifth Division, sent a telegram stating that the division took advantage of the victory to advance on Hengfeng from Yiyang and recovered the county seat on the 5th. The bandit army retreated to the border between Dexing and Yiyang. The county magistrate of Hengfeng is currently concurrently serving as the county magistrate of Yiyang. However, the essence of the county seat has been lost for a long time. The farmers in the four townships have either been turned into bandits or displaced, the fields are barren, and the houses are in ruins. The situation is very miserable. After receiving the news of the recovery of Hengcheng, the provincial government is looking for capable people to appoint as county magistrates, so as to handle the aftermath, recruit refugees, save the dying and heal the wounded, so as to restore vitality as soon as possible. Feng Yuxiang Elaborates on Political Views 76

Retreating to the Mountains to Trace the Reasons for Failure

The Way to Self-Preservation Lies in Diligent War Preparations

Discipline and Restore the Party's Democratic System

Restore Freedom and Revive the People's Movement

Zhangjiakou Correspondence: After arriving in Zhangyuan, Feng Yuxiang resided in the Boai Hospital. Recently, Feng expressed his personal thoughts and political views, which are recorded as follows:

"The general public's criticisms of me include both praise and condemnation. The things for which I am praised are what I should do and are my national obligations, and I dare not be arrogant about them. As for the criticisms, they are mainly two points: one is that I go too far in correcting wrongs, and the other is that I am prone to defection. In fact, both of these criticisms do not truly understand my mistakes. I have rarely expressed political views, so people inevitably misunderstand me. From a revolutionary standpoint, any revolution inevitably involves overthrowing the ruling class that oppresses the majority of the people. If one only blindly follows the rulers, there can be no revolution. Therefore, what I have done in the past was to overthrow the ruling class. If we consider it from the perspective of feudalistic subordination, all our revolutionary actions were defections. For example, my campaign in Langfang to suppress the restoration, my overthrow of the bribery-ridden government in Beijing, the expulsion of Puyi from the palace, and the recent wars – should reactionary gentlemen like these be permanently retained on the stage? However, I have repeatedly participated in revolutions without expressing my specific political views, because in the past, I believed that any government that violated the interests of the people and oppressed the people should be overthrown. As for what should be done after the overthrow, I would wait for the virtuous and talented people in the country to solve it. I never had the intention of seizing power for myself, so after overthrowing the bad government, I would automatically resign and invite the leaders of various factions to take over, as evidenced by the situation after the overthrow of the bribery-ridden government. I always wanted to identify the evildoers and resolve to eliminate them. After the evildoers are overthrown, good people will come. Who would have thought that after one group of evildoers left, another group of evildoers would come? Not only are those engaged in revolution exhausted, but the innocent people also suffer repeated sacrifices. This is my mistake, my past mistake of having no clear plan for the revolution. Now I realize this mistake, so in recent years, I have devoted myself to various political, economic, and social issues, as well as revolutionary theories, to seek a political solution after the revolution. As for those who accuse me of going too far in correcting wrongs, I also have an explanation. I came from a poor family and joined the army at the age of seventeen, entirely from the ranks, so I have experienced many difficulties and deeply understand the hidden pains of the lowest levels of society. Naturally, I deeply hate and resent those gentlemen who wear silk and brocade and eat delicacies but do not do their jobs properly. Naturally, I see the various injustices in society and am easily inspired to resist. This is the root cause of my repeated participation in revolutions. My ability to endure hardship also comes from this. Comparing my current life with the past, although I still wear cloth clothes and eat simple food, I feel that my personal living situation is enough. Especially for revolutionaries who aspire to save the world and help the people, why bother seeking personal enjoyment first? Therefore, I want to use my life as a standard, to raise the lives of many, many poor compatriots in society to be like mine. As for those gentlemen who live in extravagance and luxury, I also hope to reduce their living standards. In China, where production is backward, waste should not be tolerated. If the people of the whole country could live the life of an American capitalist, I would naturally not object to the enjoyment of silk and brocade. Therefore, from the perspective of a capitalist, perhaps my simple life is going too far in correcting wrongs and is not close to their human nature. If we are willing to calmly consider, if all the gentlemen in the country lived my kind of life, it would not necessarily be unhealthy. I am afraid that the health of the gentlemen in silk and brocade is not as good as mine. This is from a personal perspective. From a social perspective, if everyone lived like me, it might be possible to slightly reverse the trend of extravagance and luxury, and it might be possible to reduce the consumption of foreign goods. Moreover, frugality can foster integrity, which can reduce the number of corrupt officials. So, is my emphasis on frugality going too far in correcting wrongs, or is the emphasis on extravagance going too far? This is my past situation. As for why I now have a clear plan, since the failure of the war the year before last, I have retreated to the mountains and have had two years of quiet reflection. This has been a perfect opportunity for focused research. I often reflect on the past, trace the causes of repeated failures, and diligently read all kinds of social science books to nourish my thoughts and make me more systematic in seeking a way to transform Chinese society. Using the theories in the books, combined with my past experiences and the current social situation, I have come to two realizations: first, that to work hard for the revolutionary cause, one must have correct principles; and second, that the various current doctrines all have their strengths and weaknesses, especially regarding the initial implementation measures, which may not fully align with the needs of Chinese society today. Therefore, I am addressing the problem by reforming the system. At this critical moment of national crisis, the most ferocious of the imperialist powers, and the one that openly and continuously invades with military force, is naturally Japan. Yet the government not only does not resist, but even fails to plan for self-defense after the fact. Consider that the independence and integrity of any country cannot rely on the support of other countries. To rely on others to build a nation is to become a protectorate. Even elementary school students know this. Therefore, under the military pressure of Japan, the only way is to strive for self-reliance and survival, and it cannot be solved by simply appealing to the League of Nations. We cannot hope that the League of Nations will recover our territory or maintain our border defenses. Moreover, the officials responsible for national defense have adopted a policy of non-resistance. Why should outsiders bother to resist on our behalf? Therefore, I believe that no matter what the diplomatic situation is, we must diligently prepare for war, first making preparations to strengthen national defense. We should gather military leaders and experts to jointly formulate national defense plans and divide the country into national defense zones. All the national armies should be selected by the central government for their elite troops and stationed at important locations. The old and weak should combine with the local people to be responsible for rear transportation and local security, with the police, militia, and volunteer forces responsible. The ordnance factories should be unified and moved to the interior. These are the urgent tasks of war preparation. In past revolutionary wars, those who died for the revolution were not given compensation, the disabled were not given settlement, the wounded were not given awards, and the meritorious were not given recognition. As a result, the parents of the dead and disabled soldiers became beggars, their wives and children were scattered and displaced, and their children were sold in the market. All these facts have led to the loss of military and popular support, and this must be addressed first. All officers and soldiers, even when facing foreign insults, cannot avoid worrying about the future. Now, to inspire the morale of the army, we must first strengthen their faith and encourage their loyalty and bravery. For those who died in battle, the nation should build national shrines, and the villages should build village shrines. Their parents, wives, and children should be compensated, and the disabled should be given preferential treatment and provided with factories to support their lives. A special agency should be established, with designated personnel to handle the matter, and special funds should be allocated within a specified number of months. If the results are not effective, the personnel should be punished. This is the most important thing in war preparation. Secondly, the government should reject nepotism and favoritism, and those who have made meritorious contributions in the real revolution should be quickly identified and promoted. Restore the Party's democratic system, rectify the Party's discipline, and then the party members will be elite and their actions will be unified, so that the Party can be effective. The capital should still be moved to a suitable location to avoid the threat of imperialism. Restore the people's movement, and guarantee freedom of assembly, association, speech, and publication. Restore various people's organizations, provide them with military training, implement strict austerity policies, cut unnecessary agencies, implement financial transparency to prevent waste, and strictly formulate regulations for punishing officials for dereliction of duty and corruption to rectify officialdom. Formulate a production plan to meet the necessary consumption principles of the whole country. The state should operate foreign trade, and luxury goods should be monopolized by the state and subject to purchase restrictions. Strictly levy progressive income and inheritance taxes, and stipulate the highest salaries for civil servants and the lowest salaries for farmers and workers. Formulate social insurance laws, establish special agencies, and implement them in practice. Revise the education plan, cultivate talents needed by the country, and provide people with equal opportunities for education. All these are urgent matters that cannot be delayed. Earlier, Mr. Wang Jingwei telegraphed me and asked about my views, and this is what I advocated. Until now, I still believe that if the above points are implemented immediately, and then we actively resist Japan, there will be success. I sent a telegram in Taishan a month ago, saying that if the central government is determined to resist Japan, I and Bai Chuan are willing to go to Nanjing and sit in jail. I am willing to do so, but unfortunately, it has been delayed until now and is still in a state of suspended animation. Now the national affairs are increasingly urgent. If I do not die for the country, the country will die for me. I hope that the people of the country will work together to overcome the difficulties." (October 12)

Unprecedented Fire Disaster in Datong 77

Over Eight Hundred Houses Destroyed

Approximately Twenty People Killed and Injured

Wuhu Correspondence: Datong and Yuezhou, which belong to Tongling County in Anhui Province, are the most prosperous commercial towns along the Yangtze River in Anhui Province and the gateway to the southern Anhui counties and into Anhui Province. In the past, there were plans to establish four cities: Anqing, Wuhu, Bengbu, and Datong. The importance of its commercial location can be imagined. However, the transportation sector here received a telegram from Datong stating that a fire suddenly broke out on the Hengdi embankment on the island last night around ten o'clock. At that time, the southeast wind was strong, and the weather was dry, so in an instant, the fire had spread wildly. Fireboats on both sides of the river and the navy's Chen-class torpedo boat fire brigade rushed to the scene upon hearing the alarm. However, the fire was fanned by the wind, and fireballs were flying everywhere. As a result, from the foot of the embankment, passing through the Huainan Public Office, the post office, the road behind, the south bank of the pond, the vegetable garden behind the Ma family, and the area along the river, everywhere was on fire. The fireboats were divided to deal with the situation, and they were exhausted. Houses collapsed and walls crumbled, and the sound shook for several miles. Refugees were running east and west, with no way to escape, wailing and crying miserably, which was extremely tragic. The first battalion of the Datong Training Corps and the Marine Corps of the Chen-class torpedo boat were all armed and suppressing the scene. The fire gradually subsided at one o'clock in the midnight. When riverboats passed by the area, they still saw the sky full of fire, illuminating the river. Although it only lasted for three hours, over eight hundred houses had been destroyed. Seventy to eighty percent of the shops were burned down. The essence of the entire town was almost completely destroyed. The losses have not yet been calculated. According to the initial investigation, in addition to one old man and one child who were buried in the fire, and an unknown number of people who were burned and scorched while trying to move their belongings, there were more than ten people who fell into the river due to running carelessly in the dark or due to being overwhelmed. It was a truly tragic disaster. (October 15)

Huai River Diversion Project is Actively Underway 78

Building a Movable Dam at Hongze Lake Mouth and Dredging the Zhangfu River

Organizing Government-Owned滩地on Both Banks and Raising Public Bonds

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The Jiangsu Huai River diversion project has been progressing smoothly since it continued on September 1. According to Huang Bokui, the chief engineer of the Pukou Engineering Bureau, the Huai River diversion project was previously suspended due to financial constraints. Also, due to differing opinions on the issues of entering the Yangtze River and entering the sea, the Huai River Diversion Committee of the National Government, in order to avoid opposition from the people in the upstream and downstream areas, decided to allow both to be done at the same time. In terms of engineering, one is to dredge the Jiang Dam and the movable dam at the mouth of Hongze Lake, allowing the water from the Huai River passing through Hongze Lake to enter the sea through the Yan River and the Guan River. This can regulate the water volume of the lake and maintain a fixed amount of lake water. When the water is high, the dam is opened to divert water into the Yangtze River, and when the water is low, the dam is closed to conserve water. The second is to dredge the Zhangfu River to allow the water to flow in a straight line and smoothly into the sea, preventing it from being winding and silted up. In terms of funding, the original budget for the first phase of five years was 49 million yuan. However, the construction of the movable dam at Hongze Lake alone requires 1 million yuan in the first year. This amount differs greatly. The Huai River Diversion Committee is now starting to organize government-owned滩地on both sides of the river, so that this huge amount of funding can be shared by the people and the state. Therefore, raising funds is more convenient than before. The previous proposal to raise public bonds from the local people, with the designated funds as collateral, to facilitate turnover and relief, is expected to succeed. The Huai River Diversion and Sea Entry Engineering Bureau of this committee, originally located at Chenjiawan in Lianshui, has now moved to Qingjiangpu. In short, the committee is determined to continue working hard on the Huai River diversion and complete this huge project, which is closely related to tens of millions of people, in the shortest possible time.

(October 15)

The Northwest Reclamation Corps Advocates Thorough Development of the Northwest 79

After arriving in Baotou, the Northwest Reclamation Corps investigation team has been conducting investigations for several months. The team issued a declaration yesterday on the development of the Northwest, which is recorded as follows: "[Everyone in the country knows that today the Southeast is a land of wealth, and its material civilization can compete with Europe and America. The development of the Southeast is far more advanced than the stagnation of the Northwest. However, before the Han and Tang dynasties, the people of the Southeast had unkempt hair and tattooed bodies, and were not worthy of being compared with the advanced people of Qi and Lu. The land was barren and salty, and there were many miasmas and diseases. The people of the Northwest regarded it as a place to be feared and a place of exile for criminals. How is this different from the way the people of the Southeast view the Northwest today? The political center of gravity in ancient times was in the Northwest, and the Southeast was considered insignificant. Today, the center of gravity is in the Southeast, and the Northwest is considered irrelevant. Each is blinded by its own perspective. In fact, the Northwest and the Southeast are both parts of China's beautiful landscape. They are interdependent, each with its own strengths, and their merits cannot be distinguished. However, there is a persistent misunderstanding of this in both ancient and modern times. The investigation team's report is being edited, so there is no need to dwell on it here. However, the Northwest is isolated beyond the borders, while the doors of the Southeast are wide open. The Northwest faces the danger of emptiness, while the Southeast suffers from overcrowding. If we do not break open regional concepts, abandon feudal ideas, and take a deep look at the objective historical perspective of the world, and conduct a thorough investigation to find a reliable way forward, not only will the Northwest and the Southeast never understand each other and never have the hope of balanced development, but China will also face the danger of destruction. Therefore, the investigation team, without regard for hard work and at the cost of all sacrifices, has prepared its own resources and ventured far in the summer heat to do this investigation work. As a result, our gains are more than we had hoped for, and beyond our expectations. We initially thought that the Northwest was restricted too severely by nature and could not develop freely. Who knew that all the natural shortcomings could be easily remedied? How could we compare it to the Southeast's barren salt flats, low temperatures, miasmas, insurmountable mountains, rapidly flowing rivers with many reefs, and dangerous ocean waves, all of which cannot be overcome by human power? To develop the Northwest, we do not need to use Western material civilization's machines, and we can see results immediately. Even using our old spirit of developing the Southeast, we can achieve twice the results with half the effort. The problem with the world is that we do not know the bottom line, so sound, light, electricity, and chemistry all show amazing achievements. Once we know them, all progress is as easy as turning our hand. We now have a clear understanding of the Northwest as the Northwest. The development of the Northwest is as easy as lifting a hand or taking a step. However, the Northwest region is vast and cannot be covered in a short time. For the time being, we will start with Suiyuan and proceed step by step, with Xinjiang as the final destination. Baotou is the end of the Ping-Sui Railway, and goods from the west are concentrated here. From here, we can reach Ningxia and Xinjiang. Since we have taken the development of the Northwest as our responsibility, then after the investigation, we will naturally base our business on this. In addition to actively preparing new villages, immigrating and reclaiming land, we will also take advantage of the winter leisure time to establish a woolen mill in Baotou to help the market and establish a base for the corps, which will be used as a signal for the development of the Northwest. Once all the projects have a beginning, we will move forward until the Northwest and the Southeast coexist and prosper together. Since Qin Shi Huang immigrated 100,000 households here and built the Great Wall along the Yin Mountains to demarcate it, the Hetao area has been included in the territory since the Han and Tang dynasties and treated as the inland. However, we are not good at management, and we still treat it as a desolate and remote area, which is not as good as the Europeans and Americans who came here to preach, who regard it as a paradise and call it the Catholic Kingdom. Now, the Suiyuan Provincial Government has taken measures to cultivate soldiers, civilians, and Mongols, and this corps will also cultivate agriculture, industry, and commerce to thoroughly develop it. It is hoped that the whole country will be united, with those with wealth investing and those with strength joining the effort. Many hands make light work, and if we inspire hidden potential and strengthen national defense, we may have a chance of success. This is our declaration.]"

Shen Honglie's Plan to Prosper Qingdao 80

Expanding the City Area, Dividing into Industrial, Commercial, and Residential Zones

Expanding Roads for City Residents to Visit Scenic Spots

Qingdao Correspondence: The Rotary Club of Qingdao held a luncheon at the International Club on the 13th of this month. In addition to members, leaders from various sectors of diplomacy, industry, and commerce, both Chinese and foreign, were invited to dine together. During the luncheon, Mayor Shen Honglie gave a detailed speech on the plan to prosper Qingdao, which can be summarized as follows: "Today, I am honored that President Mei Weiliang of this club wants me to talk about my work matters with you. I am very interested, because if I speak from my own position elsewhere, I will inevitably involve politics. But today, I am purely speaking as a member, making a friendly talk and can only discuss our immediate problems, without involving other matters. Regardless of whether what I am talking about is right or wrong, you will surely forgive me and need not have many concerns. My work in Qingdao, if speaking in business terms, can be divided into two parts: livelihood and life. The livelihood part, in order to seek prosperous business, must have a considerable area. This area can be divided into two types: land and harbor. On the land side, we plan to expand the city to the line of Cangku and Damai Island, and the northwest sides within this line, about twice the size of Qingdao City, are designated as industrial and commercial areas, so that factories, shops, and all residents can gradually increase. On the harbor side, in addition to building the new Fifth Pier, we plan to gradually build other piers along the Fourth Pier and try to fill in the beach connecting the Fourth Pier and Sifang, turning it into industrial, commercial, and pier land. As the sea and land gradually expand in this way, the city's industry and commerce will surely develop day by day, and the livelihood of Chinese and foreign citizens can be resolved. On the life side, in order to seek a comfortable life for the citizens, there must be a scenic and elegant residence. In recent years, the city has gradually developed, and there is already the problem of expensive land and crowded people. In the future, we plan to gradually equip all roads and water supply and drainage systems in the area along the coast from Zhanshan East to Damai Island, facing the sea and backing the mountains, about equal to the size of Qingdao City, and develop it into a residential area, specially for high-class men and women to live in. After the road network is completed in the future, the farthest point can reach the city in about an hour, and the air is clear, the scenery is beautiful, the seawater bathing beach is beautiful, and the convenience of living is better than living in the city. As for Laoshan, which is a scenic spot in the city, although it is far from the city, it can be used for leisure tours. We plan to first build roads in various scenic spots in the mountain area to connect them and facilitate transportation. Then, we will promote the construction of hotels or villa villages in scenic places. The tap water can be filled with mountain spring water, and electric lights can be set up according to the needs of various departments. Not only can the people of the city enjoy themselves at any time, but also the summer resort tourists can enjoy the mountains and rivers at their own leisure. In this way, we have this adjustment in our lives, and we will not feel dry and cramped. In the future, the customers who patronize the city may also increase because of this, and the business of our store's livelihood department will surely prosper as a result. In addition, the supplementary matters of tap water and telephones are also important issues in the city. The short-term solution for tap water has been decided, and the water volume can be increased by 100,000 tons per month before March next year. Based on past experience, there will be a surplus in two years. As for the telephone bureau, it is directly under the Ministry of Communications and is not within the scope of the city, but the telephone bureau here has decided to add 400 units before April next year, no matter what, and reduce the installation price to comfort the desire of the Chinese and foreign people in the city. These two levels are also related to the master plan of life, so I will mention them together. The above is the business plan of our store, but the capital that the enemy has is only spirit and labor, which is very limited. This club brings together various talents and is intended to be a place for mutual research, and both livelihood and life are necessary for everyone, so I hope that you will give more suggestions so that we can achieve the above goals. Then, not only will our store gradually prosper, but also your livelihood and life problems can be solved satisfactorily." (October 14)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 82

Joint Meeting of Water and Land Police Forces for City and Suburb Defense: As the winter season approaches, winter defense measures for the city and suburbs should be implemented according to established plans. Yesterday, the County Public Security Bureau, recognizing the vastness and importance of the city and suburban area's defense, convened the first joint defense meeting at the Public Security Bureau. Nine individuals attended, including members of the Water Patrol Team, Police Team, patrol officers from the four districts, inspectors, and the heads of the Yu and Xu sections of the Public Security Bureau. During the meeting, defense measures and district assignments were decided. The district assignments were as follows: The area east of the Wazi Lane straight line, up to the southeast city gate and the vicinity outside the southeast gate, will be patrolled by the Police Team. The area west of the Wazi Lane straight line, up to the northwest city gate, will be patrolled by the chief of the first police precinct and four detective officers. The area outside the east gate will be patrolled jointly by the chief of the fourth police precinct and two detective officers, in cooperation with the Police Team. The area outside the north gate will be patrolled by officers from the Water Patrol Team. The area outside the west gate, encompassing the jurisdictions of the second and third police precincts, will be patrolled by the respective patrol officers, with additional patrol support from the Public Security Bureau's special task force police officers and detectives. In the event of temporary incidents in any district, regardless of the area, assistance will be dispatched immediately upon notification. Notifications have been sent to the relevant water and land police agencies for compliance.

The Chinese Athletic Association Performs in Songjiang Public Stadium: This is the only organization in our county that promotes sports. They have specially hired the renowned instructor Fu Xiushan for training, achieving notable results. Recently, to raise funds for construction, Mr. Fu invited the Jin Shaoshan and his entire troupe from the Chinese Martial Arts Athletic Association to perform in Songjiang. The program includes astonishing feats such as driving a car over a person's body and flying through lead wires. Performances started today, with both day and night shows. Tickets are priced low to encourage wider participation and promote martial arts.

Suzhou 83

Police Recklessly Open Fire, Killing and Injuring Multiple People: At 8 PM tonight, two individuals were discovered walking on the roof of the residence of Ye Boliang, a wealthy resident of Fulangzhong Lane, Shengjiating (from a wealthy family in Dongting East Mountain). Neighbors, suspecting a robbery, sounded the alarm. Police rushed to the scene, and a fire brigade also mistakenly arrived, thinking it was a fire. A state of chaos ensued. Police recklessly opened fire, killing a passerby named Chen Huasheng (an employee of a fruit store) on the spot. Zhu, a resident, was seriously injured, and Chen Desheng, Zhu Jin'si, Xu Youfu, Xu Quanlin, and Sun Yonglin sustained minor injuries and were taken to the hospital for treatment. A suspect named Guo Xianglin (from Chaozhou) was apprehended by the police and is currently under strict interrogation at the police station.

Taicang 84

Pond Construction Committee Inspects Seawall: The sections of the seawall in Li River, Daotang Temple, Parade Ground, Yanglinkou, and other areas within the county's jurisdiction have been completed on schedule. Dong Xiujia, Director of the Construction Department, specially dispatched technician Zhang Youbin to join Zhu Kaichou of the Jiangnan Pond Construction Rehabilitation Committee and Qiu Xijue, Director of the Pond Construction Office, to inspect and accept the Xu Liujing section on the morning of the 14th at 8 AM. They also inspected other sections and have since returned to the provincial capital to report.

Elementary School Principal Attempts Suicide, Rescued: Due to financial difficulties, the county has been unable to pay the schools for four and a half months. On the 14th, Wu Yun, principal of Penglai Elementary School, went to the Education Bureau to request funds but was unsuccessful. Overwhelmed by financial worries, he attempted suicide by jumping into the Lujia River. Fortunately, someone noticed him early and quickly rescued him, and he is not in critical condition.

Wuxi 85

All Silk Factories Resumed Work Today: The county-wide silk factory strike has seen considerable progress since He Yushu, Li Mingyang, and Zhang Gongren came to Wuxi to mediate. Work was originally scheduled to resume on the 16th, but the factory owners requested a slight delay to prepare for the resumption. Therefore, all factories resumed work uniformly on the 17th. The mediation meeting originally scheduled to be held at the county government yesterday has been postponed until after the resumption of work. Yesterday morning at 10 AM, factory owner representatives Cheng Bingruo, Xue Shouhuan, Xie Youan, and over twenty others visited Commissioners He, Li, and Zhang at the Railway Hotel to report on the strike's progress and the silk factories' recent situation. The commissioners explained the provincial government's intentions and urged them to resume work immediately. The factory representatives stated that they were willing to resume work, but that they had attempted to resume work three times between the 11th and 13th, but were stopped due to disturbances by female workers. If they were to comply with the order to resume work immediately, they feared that more accidents would occur, causing greater losses to the factories and affecting public order. They felt this point should be considered. Commissioner He said that the provincial government had sent security soldiers to Wuxi for protection. If anyone intentionally incited or attempted to disrupt the situation, they would be severely punished and shot on the spot. Therefore, this point should not be overly concerned about. After a long discussion, it was decided that work would resume uniformly on the 17th. After the factory representatives left, they held a temporary members' meeting at 3 PM to report on the meeting with Commissioners He, Li, and Zhang, and then sent notices to their colleagues, stating that they would resume work uniformly on the morning of the 17th. At the same time, the Silk Factory Industry Workers' Union also held a representative meeting, where Commissioners Li and Zhang spoke, stating that anyone who intentionally disobeyed the guidance would be held fully responsible for the labor unrest and would be severely punished. The representatives then made three demands: (1) Wages of 57 cents, and full wages for employees and silkworm raisers. (2) Work hours limited to six hours up and six hours down. (3) The factory owners would be responsible for the post-incident care of female workers injured in the conflict under the Gongyun Bridge on the 13th. Commissioners Li and Zhang accepted these demands. The representatives then decided to comply with the order to resume work on the 17th. At 4:30 PM, Wu Dexin, Director of the Public Security Bureau, believing that it was necessary to question Chen Mengqi, the worker representative from the Chuansantai Silk Factory, about the labor unrest, ordered two detectives to bring Chen to the bureau for questioning and then ordered him to return. However, it was rumored that Chen had been arrested, so members of the Gongyun Association petitioned Zhang Gongren of the Provincial Party Committee, but the misunderstanding was soon cleared up. It was also heard that when Commissioners He and Li came to Wuxi, the provincial government had issued a formal order that anyone who disrupted order or incited labor unrest could be shot on the spot. Furthermore, Gu Zhenglun, the commander of the Gendarmerie, had also issued an order to Wuxi, instructing them to use military law when necessary to suppress those who disrupted public order in order to maintain local security.

Gang of Kidnappers Smashed, Hostage Rescued: In Xue Dian Township, Da He Tou area, District 12 (Biaobeishi) of the county, Weng Zhendong, a wealthy man of 22 years old with over 400 mu of good farmland and substantial wealth, was suddenly robbed on the night of the 29th of last month at 1 AM. He was robbed of over 1,000 silver dollars' worth of clothing and taken away. His family came to the city to report to the County Bureau, requesting the rescue of the hostage. Wu Dexin, Director of the Public Security Bureau, considered the case significant and, as instructed by the County Magistrate, offered a reward for information. However, no news had been received for over half a month. On the 10th of this month, Weng's family received two letters from the kidnappers, demanding 3,000 yuan in cash by the morning of yesterday (15th) at Furong Mountain, or the hostage would be killed. Weng's mother, He, felt that the kidnappers' attitude was too harsh to deal with, and had no choice but to report to Zhu Meiji, head of the 8th District Security Corps. After receiving the report, Chief Zhu immediately dispatched militiamen disguised as farmers and ambushed the foot of Furong Mountain. At the same time, Weng's younger brother, Feng Nan, and a farmhand went to the meeting place and contacted the two kidnappers. Chief Zhu surrounded them from behind while they were talking and captured the two kidnappers. After interrogation, he sent militiamen to escort the two kidnappers to the corps headquarters for detention. He then personally led detectives to Tushan Bay, near Xicang, based on the information provided by the kidnappers, and arrested 14 major criminals, including Xu Fengchi and Zhuang Shigen. They also rescued the hostage, Weng Zhendong, and brought them all back to the corps headquarters for temporary detention. They plan to submit a written report to the county government today for legal action and to issue warrants for the arrest of the gang leaders for severe punishment.

Changzhou 86

Kidnapper Gong Quanfa Executed by Firing Squad: Song Maozhao, deputy head of the 8th District Security Corps of Wu County, captured Gong Quanfa, a habitual offender of kidnapping and robbery, in Gongjia Village in September of this year. He was handed over to the county for trial, and it was confirmed that he was an accomplice of Taibao Ashu, the head of the Taihu bandits who had been executed, and had committed numerous crimes. He was sentenced to death, and the provincial order was approved on the 15th. The criminal was taken to the execution ground after verifying his identity and executed by firing squad.

Business Tax Officially Implemented: Due to the impact of the Shanghai War, the spring and summer business taxes in Wu County were difficult to collect. Recently, Lu Fengtai was appointed as the director, and after completing the investigation procedures, the tax amounts payable by the various businesses were mostly ascertained, and collection officially started yesterday (15th), with a public announcement made.

Zhenjiang 87

Zhu Peide and Wife Tour Jinshan and Jiaoshan: Zhu Peide, admiring the scenery of Jinshan and Jiaoshan, took advantage of the high autumn and clear weather to travel by car from Nanjing to Zhenjiang at 7 AM yesterday with his wife. To avoid social obligations, only Director Li Mingyang, an old friend, was notified in advance. After Zhu arrived in Zhenjiang, he stayed at the provincial residence, and Director Li arranged for Director Jiang to take care of everything and sent a naval warship to escort them to Jiaoshan for sightseeing. All District Chiefs File Complaint Against County Magistrate: It is said that County Magistrate Li recently accompanied Xie Fuqiu of the Provincial Committee to inspect the security corps in various districts. This stirred up the public outrage of all district chiefs. Bandits Rob Da Lu Township: Since the beginning of autumn, bandit activity in the four rural areas of the county has been rampant, with kidnapping and looting occurring daily. A few days ago, several dozen bandits armed with guns came to Da Lu Township and went to the homes of over ten farmers, including Chen Zengrong, to search. They looted silver dollars, clothing, rice, and other items. The losses are said to be quite substantial.

Pinghu 89

Automobile Accident on Highway: Since the opening of the Shanghai-Hangzhou highway, there have been two accidents on the Zayan section, resulting in the deaths of two children. A few days ago, near the Liuzhai residence of Liangzhuangxiang Fork Road Bridge, dozens of cars sped by in succession. Many villagers stood by the roadside to watch. Jia Youchang, an apprentice in a woodworking shop, crossed the highway in the dust and was knocked down and crushed, suffering serious injuries and bleeding profusely. The car did not stop to rescue him but sped west. It was also reported that a car overturned on the seawall four or five li south of Haiyan, and all the occupants were seriously injured.

Silk Fabric Merchants Still Import Japanese Goods: Shenghexiang Silk Fabric Store in front of the North Temple previously swore an oath to the Anti-Japanese Association not to import Japanese goods. However, the owner of the store has been secretly dealing with Japanese merchants. Ignoring his oath, he recently sent his staff to the Japanese merchant Taishan Yoko in Shanghai to purchase five pieces of Qiaoqi brand velveteen. That night, they were transported by the Qingji night shift boat to Pinghu. The boat was intercepted by the local Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in Zhujing, and the goods were confiscated. Yesterday, Shen Hongfei, a clerk from the association, came to Pinghu to explain the situation to the Anti-Japanese Association and requested that a fine be imposed as a warning.

Letter from Wuxi County Girls' High School 90

To the esteemed Editor of Shenbao:

We are writing in response to the news item published in your local news column on October 15th, titled "Wuxi County Girls' High School Cook Complains of Injustice in Prison." After careful review, we find that the content of this article is completely inconsistent with the facts and is truly shocking. The food expenses for our school's students and faculty were determined through mutual agreement and cannot be changed arbitrarily. When settling accounts this time, the calculation was based on 17 cents per day per person, exactly as agreed, and there was absolutely no reduction of 2 cents. The facts are clear and the accounts are available for verification. As for the claim that Mr. Guo Zhengmo's demand for compensation was not met and that Mr. Guo was slandered, these are vicious and baseless accusations. They are the words of a rogue and not worth refuting. Furthermore, this case is currently being handled by the court and will be decided according to law. Therefore, it is not necessary for our school to say anything further. However, we fear that a lack of understanding of the true situation will lead to confusion and rumors. Therefore, we have prepared this letter to correct the record.

Respectfully,

Wuxi County Girls' High School

Donghua Overwhelms Strong Opponent 91

Wins Initial Battle Two to One Against the "Lax"

Chinese and Western Goalkeeping Performances Amaze the Entire Stadium

This year's Donghua team is truly well-rounded in talent and strong in strength. Yesterday, they made their first appearance in the Western Football Club's A-League, facing the brave and skilled "Lax." The earth-shattering battle captivated over 12,000 spectators from both the northern and southern parts of the country. At the end of 90 minutes, the referee announced the ceasefire, with a score of two to one, resulting in a victory for Donghua. The referee was Stanwa, and Donghua's honorary doctor was Dr. Fang Jiacheng.

Clash of the Chinese and Western Goalkeepers 94

Yesterday's battle, instead of being called a contest between Donghua and "Lax," would be better described as a contest of skills between the two Chinese and Western goalkeepers. Why? Zhou Xianyan is undoubtedly a first-class figure, and Tewit is also a leader in his field. Both were under the sharp fire of the opponent and endured extremely difficult circumstances. They both showed their skills, resisted all kinds of clever tactics, and ultimately emerged victorious. Zhou Xianyan's strength is stronger than Tewit's, which has been powerfully proven.

A Clear Distinction on the Merit List 95

The Donghua team deployed its lineup, but lacked the key inner defender Li Ning. As a result, Feng Lianyou was moved to inner defense, Tu Kaiyuan played center, Yang Renwei filled Tu's position, and Guan Xun'an and Wu Youliang remained in their original positions. Even with this small change, the interior sometimes felt shaky. However, amidst the turmoil, we were able to find loyal and devoted individuals, such as Feng Yunyou, who played both inner and outer defense, and whose iron hooves terrified the enemy. Wu Youliang has shown remarkable progress, showing the style of Sun Sijing and making great strides forward. Tu and Guan also fulfilled their duties. Yang's performance as a forward was not his usual skill, but he improved in the second half. Wan Xianghua has a great heart and advances like a lone horse among thousands, often with amazing results. It is a pity that the central generals were always hampered by internal panic and could not unite against the outside world. Otherwise, many more goals could have been added to the record. Li Yichen's shooting, combined with Chen Hongguang's agility and Chen Jiaqiu's liveliness, added the finishing touches, but due to internal turmoil, they could not exert their full strength. Chen Yutian was not in good form and did not contribute much. He will have to wait for another opportunity to redeem himself. How was Zhou Xianyan? As mentioned above, in short, he is the number one hero in Donghua's victory.

"Lax" Talk about "Lax" again, Tewit's defense of the iron gate was a great contribution. Central defender Maeda handled the situation with ease. The inner and outer lines were interwoven. The inner defense line was usually tied up on both flanks of Donghua, so it was very active. The central three forwards truly showed their exceptional talent, but the two wings were just so-so, and right winger Beiker showed some improvement, because his monitor was not his opponent.

Deciding the Outcome in Ninety Minutes 96

First Half At the start of the battle, Donghua launched three consecutive attacks. Chen Hongguang headed the ball once, and Li Yichen headed it again, but both were ineffective. Li also kicked the ball wide. "Lax" showed its strength, and Atige was the first to test the goal, but retreated without success. Afterwards, the forwards on both sides launched fierce shots, and the two Chinese and Western goalkeepers mustered their spirits and resisted with all their strength. It was truly impossible to break through, a sight to behold. Donghua conceded first, but it was not the goalkeeper's fault. The goalkeeper was blocked by a rush of players, exposing the goal, and the ball flashed in from Atige's foot. After the initial shock, the spectators saw Wan Xianghua on the left wing take a lone horse deep into the enemy's territory, and the enemy's defenses collapsed. A pass was sent into the center, and Li Yichen swept it into the goal. The sound of cheers overflowed the stadium. At the end of the first half, the score was tied at one to one.

Second Half Wan Xianghua made an amazing move first. Chen Yutian's shot was weak, and the goalkeeper easily picked it up. Wan made a second contribution. Li Yichen was in the right place and kicked the ball in. The goalkeeper was caught off guard, and the iron gate fell. Donghua took the lead by two to one. After that, there were storms in front of both goals, but thanks to the efforts of the goalkeepers, any shot was difficult to score. "Lax" was in trouble and surrounded Donghua, launching fierce attacks, but the defense was effective, and their wishes were not fulfilled. In the end, Donghua still won by two to one.

China's failure to win one of the three relay races was the key to losing the championship. Although China's triple jump, in which it was very confident, only resulted in Xiao Dinghua taking third place and scoring two points, this was also China's fatal weakness. Although China's failure to win the championship in this International Games cannot escape the above-mentioned reasons, instead of blaming it on bad luck, it is better to say that our results are not as good as others. Almost all of the champions in all track events were won by British athletes, and British athletes did not excel in any field events. They relied solely on their outstanding track and field talent to win the championship, which is sufficient proof of their strength in track and field events. The Chinese athletes should increase the number of experienced coaches and devise strategies on how to fight and win. Looking at the results this time, most of them were created by foreign athletes. After this painful experience, can the Chinese people not make extra efforts? Last night, at the start of the closing speech, Mayor Wu said that he hoped that the results of the fourth International Games next year would be even better. The reporter said that he hoped that the Chinese athletes would make up for their mistakes and not let others take the credit again next year. Perhaps today's failure will be tomorrow's success. Let us all encourage each other.

Short and Long Distances 101

100 Meters: English Runner Dispute - The two main British athletes, Waller and Hurst, both achieved a time of 11.3 seconds in the preliminary rounds the day before, tying for first place. Unexpectedly, after being penalized twice for false starts in the final, the British team protested the referee's decision. After several negotiations, it was still decided to use the preliminary round results (details in another article). It was generally believed that they would surely win. China and England each had three athletes competing, making the competition exceptionally fierce. Ultimately, our team's performance was not as good, and we had to concede defeat. Waller won the championship with a time of only 11.2 seconds, Hurst came in second, and Wang Jihuai and Hao Chunde tied for third.

200 Meters: Fu Jincheng Strives - Fu Jincheng's time of 23.3 seconds in the preliminary round was the best. Hurst, who was defeated by Fu, was known not to have exerted his full strength and was only seeking to qualify. Therefore, the competition between Fu and Hurst in yesterday's final was highly anticipated by the audience. As expected, Hurst won first place with 23.6 seconds, Fu Jincheng fought hard to secure second place, Horace came in third, and Arash came in fourth. In the first 100 meters of the race, the American Arash unleashed his power and almost overwhelmed all the other competitors.

400 Meters: Excellent Performance - The Englishman Eckel achieved an outstanding time of 52.2 seconds in the preliminary round. It was generally believed that he would undoubtedly win the championship in yesterday's final. Unexpectedly, his time was reduced by another two-tenths of a second compared to the preliminary round, demonstrating his profound skills. England won a total of ten points in this race, and their momentum was overwhelming. The Chinese Customs Superintendent, Guan Changfa, gave it his all, but only managed to secure fourth place. This was due to a significant difference in skill, and it was impossible to demand more.

800 Meters: Long-Legged Xian is Fierce - The British "Long-Legged Immortal," Besant, won the 1,500-meter championship the day before with a time of 4 minutes and 21.4 seconds. Yesterday, he once again delivered a beautiful performance, winning the 800-meter championship. His time was only 2 minutes and 4.8 seconds, which was highly satisfactory. Upon investigation, apart from Yu Xiwei, who once reached 2 minutes and 1 second, the rest of our country's athletes are far behind.

The Chinese participants, Dong Shuzhao and Xia Xianzhuan, secured the third and fourth positions, respectively, and their performance was also quite strong. The second place went to the American, Breckenridge.

10,000 Meters: Wang Zhenglin Takes Second - The British team has many sprinters, but unexpectedly, they also have a long-distance runner like Kenner Tai, who runs like a celestial horse in the 10,000-meter race. As a result, Wang Zhenglin finished behind Kenner Tai by 250 meters, settling for second place. Fifteen people started the race. In the initial 1,000 meters, Ken and Lu Bingsheng were neck and neck in the lead, with Wang Zhenglin and Jin Zhongkang following closely behind by 30 feet. In the next 2,000 meters, Ken and Lu gradually increased their speed, and Wang's distance widened slightly. The two Russians gradually overtook Jin Zhongkang. At the 3,000-meter mark, Ken and Lu's pace seemed to slow down, while Wang Zhenglin closely followed behind, with a distance of about 50 feet. After Jin Zhongkang fell behind, he stepped forward at the 5,000-meter mark. After running 6,000 meters, Kenner Tai remained unchanged, and Lu Bingsheng began to fall behind. Jin Zhongkang had moved up to fourth place, behind Wang. At this point, the situation had become a four-way battle between China and England. At 6,400 meters, Wang Zhenglin surged ahead of Lu Bingsheng and was about to compete with Kenner Tai. However, in the final 3,000 meters, although Wang surpassed Lu Bingsheng, his distance from Kenner Tai continued to widen. At 8,000 meters, Ken was already 50 meters ahead of Wang, while Wang was 100 meters ahead of Lu Bingsheng, and Jin Zhongkang was another 200 meters behind. Wang's speed could not increase, and it became impossible to surpass Ken. Lu Bingsheng had once caught up and ran alongside Wang in the final 1,000 meters, but soon fell behind. By the time Ken reached the finish line, Wang was still 250 meters away. Although Wang did not chase after him, he still gave his final sprint to the end, which was met with applause from the entire stadium. Lu Bingsheng finished third, about ten yards behind Wang, and Jin Zhongkang finished fourth, another 100 meters behind. Although the other athletes were not selected, they all reached the finish line one by one. Kenner Tai maintained the same speed throughout and his expression did not change. His time of 34 minutes and 49.5 seconds was rare here and had to be praised. Wang's failure was clearly due to a lack of physical strength.

Two Types of Hurdles 102

High Hurdles: Xiao and Chen Suffer a Crushing Defeat - Chen Ling had set a national record of 16.4 seconds in the Chinese preliminary round. It was unexpectedly hoped that he would steadily win first place in this international competition. However, it was not known that there was a person named Waller in the English team, who had won the 100-meter championship with a time of 11.2 seconds. His time in the high hurdles preliminary round was also 16.4 seconds, preventing Chen Ling from having the sole honor of setting the record. However, it was expected that Chen Ling would compete with Waller for the win, but Waller took the lead and Xiao Dinghua followed closely behind, while Chen Ling was in third place, fighting to the end. The order remained the same, with Xiao finishing second by a step. Upon investigation, Xiao and Chen are famous high hurdles athletes in our country, and their defeat by the English team was unexpected.

100 Meter Dispute 106

Forgiving English Athletes Unfamiliar with the Rules

A dispute arose during the first event of yesterday's opening ceremony, the 100-meter final. The reason was that the English athletes seemed to lack training in the starting procedure. After the starter called "On your marks" and "Set," they did not wait for the two-minute interval and rushed forward after the "Set" command. The starter followed the rules and judged it as a false start. According to the rules, two false starts would result in disqualification. The English athletes, Waller and Hochter, both had two false starts in a row. The starter followed the rules and disqualified them, but the English athletes, unfamiliar with the rules, refused to obey and argued forcefully, refusing to accept the judgment. After much debate, the chief referee made concessions and allowed them to participate, counting the two false starts as only one, on the grounds that they were unfamiliar with the rules and deserved forgiveness. However, it was stated that this would be strictly enforced from then on and no exceptions would be made. The matter was thus resolved by skirting around the issue.

Hao Gengsheng Discusses the Success of the North China Games 109

Four Things Worth Commemorating

- The Next Games Will Be Held in Taiyuan, with Qingdao as a Backup

Hao Gengsheng, Executive Committee Member of the North China Sports Federation and Director of Physical Education at Qingdao University, served as the chief referee in this North China Games. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday and will travel to Beijing today or tomorrow to attend a meeting of the Ministry of Education's Sports Committee. He discussed the successful state of this North China Games as follows: Hao said that this North China Games was generally very successful, and the results were excellent, breaking several national records. There were four things worth commemorating: (1) The North China Sports Federation did not stop working due to the national crisis; (2) The political leaders of North China have a deep understanding of sports; (3) In this North China Games, each province and city had ten representatives performing traditional Chinese martial arts, which did not conflict with other competitions, and can be said to have integrated Chinese and Western sports, taking the first step in implementing the resolutions of the National Sports Conference; (4) The athletes' spirit of compliance with the law is commendable. Even though Mr. Zhang Boling could not serve as the chief referee due to domestic affairs, they did not dispute the outcome and valued the spirit of rules and regulations. If this sporting spirit is promoted and expanded, it will not only be a good phenomenon in the Chinese sports world, but also an unparalleled good phenomenon for the Chinese nation. The next Games will be held in Taiyuan, accepting the invitation of the Shanxi representatives. However, Taiyuan needs to build a new stadium, and it is unknown whether the provincial government can accept it. An answer should be received within a month. Otherwise, the Games will be moved to Qingdao. As for the rumors of the Games being held in Peiping (Beijing), there is no such thing.

Local News

Postal Workers' Anti-Japanese Martyrs

Memorial Meeting Held Yesterday

Held at the Youth Propaganda Corps in the Morning

More Than 600 Representatives from All Walks of Life Attended

The National Postal Workers' General Union held a memorial service for the anti-Japanese martyrs of postal workers from all over the country at the Youth Propaganda Corps in Xiaoximen at 9:00 am yesterday. More than 600 representatives from the Central Party Headquarters and various agencies and groups in the city attended. The atmosphere was extremely tragic and solemn. Venue Arrangement: A decorated archway was erected at the entrance of the venue, with a white cloth banner in the middle that read "Memorial Service for Anti-Japanese Martyrs of Postal Workers from All Over the Country." The couplets on both sides read, "Righteousness Reaches the Clouds, Eternal Fame Manifests Loyalty," and "Spirit Devours the Mountains and Seas, A Thousand Autumns of Postal History Comfort the Loyal Souls." Wreaths of mourning flowers were everywhere. On the stage hung the words "Sacrifice for the Public," and in the center were the portraits of the anti-Japanese martyrs Pan Jiaji, Lu Chunhua, Chen Zude, and the martyrs Chen Fangxiang, Fu Xiude, Feng Wancang, Su Pincai, Ti Jiachen, and others. The portrait of the National Revolutionary Leader and the Party and National Flags were hung on the platform. To the west of the stage were the relatives of the martyrs. The entire venue was decorated in a very solemn and tragic manner. The Municipal Public Security Bureau specially dispatched a squad of armed police officers from the First Squad of the Fifth Detachment of the Police Brigade, led by Detachment Leader Wang Shaozhou, to be on strict guard around the venue. Director Tang of the Second District Branch sent Inspector Wang to lead the police to protect the venue. The Postal Workers' Boy Scouts, led by Coach Shen Fu, maintained order at the meeting.

Participating Representatives: Wang Qi from the Central Party Headquarters, Wang Diwen from the Central Mass Movement Committee, Zhang Xiaotong from the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters, Chen Junyi from the Municipal Government, Xie Baochen from the Directorate General of Posts, Postal Director Zha Peilin, Wang Songwu from the Postal Administration, Bao Sheng and Wang Youhui from the Garrison Headquarters, Xu Dehai from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Li Yongxiang from the General Labor Union, Sun Mingqi from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Zhang Yichen from the Citizens' Union, Wang Honghui from the All-Road Merchants' Association, Zhu Jikuan and Zhu Shengsheng from the National Postal Workers' General Union, Hu Xiongding from Jiaotong University, and Zhou Xuexiang, Shao Xubai, Long Peiyun, Ye Xianggao, Li Mengnan from various labor unions, as well as Su Pincai, Chen Fangxiang, Cheng Long, Zhuang Jiliang, Wang Xingfa, and Northeast postal worker Li Weixin and other relatives of the deceased, totaling more than 600 people. When guests entered the venue, they were adorned with a yellow silk flower and a piece of black gauze by receptionists. (Photos taken by Wang Kai Photo Studio)

Memorial Ceremony: The meeting was announced at 10:00 am, and the ceremony was as follows: (1) Playing of mourning music; (2) All stand at attention; (3) Singing of the Party song; (4) Bowing three times to the Party and National Flags and the portrait of the National Revolutionary Leader; (5) Bowing three times to the portraits of the martyrs; (6) Reading the National Revolutionary Leader's will; (7) Ringing the alarm bell thirty-six times; (8) Silent tribute for three minutes to mourn the martyrs; (9) Chief officiant Lu Jingshi, assistant officiants Zhu Xuefan and Zhang Kechang, took their positions and performed the sacrificial rites; (10) Offering wreaths; (11) Reading the memorial text, Zhao Shusheng; (12) Representatives from the Central Government and various agencies and groups in the city offered sacrifices, followed by speeches from the chairman and representatives. Finally, slogans were shouted and the meeting adjourned.

Chief Officiant's Speech: Chief Officiant Lu Jingshi delivered a speech, saying that the union held the memorial service to give condolences to the postal martyrs from all over the country, and expressed gratitude for the presence of the delegates from the Central Government, and from all organizations from all walks of life. These eight martyrs were ordinary workers, but they knew the national crisis and sacrificed everything for the country. This is worthy of commemoration, and it adds a glorious page to our history of postal workers' resistance against Japan. It also adds a glorious record to the history of the postal workers' movement. But when we look back at the current situation in our country, we are filled with sorrow. Those soldiers who are supported by the people do not know how to defend against foreign enemies, but specialize in civil wars. All we see is the melee of the warlords, such as Lu Zhonghan Liu, and the two Lius in Sichuan. How do these warlords, who do not know the country but only know how to fight for power, compare with our martyred postal workers? Therefore, if we want to save the country, we must first overthrow the warlords. His speech was extremely sad and painful. Then, Zhu Xuefan, the captain of the Postal Workers' War Zone Ambulance Team, reported on the martyrs' life stories and the tragic circumstances of their martyrdom, which moved people to tears. Subsequently, Wang Qi, the representative of the Central Government, Zhang Xiaotong, the representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Li Yongxiang, the representative of the General Labor Union, delivered speeches, which were mostly sad and painful. Due to the length of the speeches, they are omitted.

Memorial Text of the General Assembly: On October 16, the 21st year of the Republic of China, the National Postal Workers' General Union, respectfully led all postal workers, with the ceremony of incense, flowers, and purity, to offer sacrifices to the anti-Japanese martyred comrades, Martyr Chen Zude, Martyr Pan Jiaji, Martyr Chen Chunhua, Martyr Chen Fangxiang, Martyr Su Pincai, Martyr Yang Jiachen, Martyr Fu Xiude. The spirit of the words say, "We Chinese people, with etiquette and clothing, strong neighbors show violence, tigers watch and eagles fly, deep pain and great trauma, national shame can be forgotten, heaven has not repented of the disaster, the enemy atmosphere is rampant, the Northeast is lost, and we are deeply hesitant, the Songhu smoke of war, and the rise of panic, sheltering the martyrs, the style is upright, the spirit is vast, the party is outstanding, the country's good, or loyal to its duties, the ambition is pure and the behavior is fragrant, or encouraging the Rong, regardless of the length, with the same hatred for the enemy, swearing to drive away tigers and wolves, boiling blood and sincerity, enduring hardships, guns and bullets, my power is increasing, wolf smoke and fire, my martial arts are increasing, hair is split, anger devours the eight wildernesses, the same way leads to the same goal, in order to plan for relief, alas, how can we expect bad news to fly, all for the country's death, hate the throat of the river, ambition, draw straw to mourn, assign the soul to be sad, offer the spirit of the sword, mourn the vastness of the spring, may the martyrs, beautiful for the sun and the moon, the doctrine is glorious, as bright as stars, showing the constitution, the heroic soul and spirit, should be passed down for thousands of years, the high mountains are steep, the flowing water is soup, the style of the martyrs, the mountains are high and the water is long, alas, alas, Shangxiang,"

Family Response: After the representatives finished their speeches, Pan Gan, the representative of the martyrs' families, gave a reply. He said that the martyrdom of the martyrs in resisting the enemy was a common occurrence. In this autumn of national crisis, all citizens should rise up to resist foreign enemies and sacrifice their lives for the country, which is the inherent duty of citizens.
