Someone suggested to the Abolish War Association

Casting iron statues of those who engage in civil war

Select important places in the city to erect them

The General Assembly of the Abolish Civil War League received a letter from He Jixiang of the First Municipal Experimental Primary School yesterday, which said, "To open with respect, abolishing civil war is the unanimous desire of the people of the whole country today, and it is also a prerequisite for us to open up a national lifeline today. How can we achieve the goal of abolishing civil war? What effective methods can be used to effectively stop the warlords' civil war? This is a major issue at present. When your association was established, it formulated many plans and announced them to the people of the country. After your association started to discuss the plans to abolish civil war, there were many different opinions. However, in reality, most of them were just empty talk on paper. How many of them can achieve practical results? When the Second Chen dispute in Guangdong arose, did your association not send telegrams and dispatch representatives to Guangdong to persuade both sides? But where is its real effect? Now the Han Liu dispute in Shandong has arisen again, and your association has once again persuaded, but the dispute remains the same. Recently, it was reported that Mao Wang in Qianzhong is about to meet with swords and soldiers. I guess your association will only persuade once again. In addition, what further sanctions will be taken is beyond the reach of your association. This is not to blame your association, because what your association can show to the people of the country today is only empty appeals. Fundamentally, there is no real power that can slightly curb the ambition of those warlords who are addicted to war. We are firm and discuss it. If we want to thoroughly eliminate the warlords today, there is no other way than revolution. The second is the method of passive non-cooperation, which can also slightly kill the warlords' arrogance. However, with the strength and organization of the people today, this level is also difficult to achieve. Therefore, today, if we want to talk emptily about abolishing civil war, without fundamentally seeking a solution, no matter what kind of strategy, we can only return to failure and will never achieve the slightest effect. The past events are clear, and they can be used as a clear proof. However, there is only one thing that is worthy of our efforts. What is that? It is to cast iron statues of those who engage in civil war in order to expose their ugliness. The idea of casting statues has a long history. When Qi caused disaster to Su, Shanghai once proposed to cast statues for them, but it was not actually implemented. However, it has attracted much attention, which shows its profound impact. I believe that in the future, those who engage in civil war, no matter who they are, will not ask who is right and who is wrong. Your association will first persuade them, and if they do not listen to the persuasion, you will cast several iron statues for both sides and explain the reasons for casting the statues. The cast statues will be erected in important places in the city to be唾罵 by all and to bear a bad name forever. Shanghai is the largest metropolis in our country. What it sees and hears will inevitably affect the whole country. Those evil warlords, although they are arrogant and invincible, if they have a little conscience, they will inevitably feel ashamed when they see this, and they will learn from the past to avoid future mistakes. Although this matter is small, its effect is great. Therefore, I would like to present it to your association, and I respectfully ask you to adopt it."

To Go to Europe for Medical Treatment in a Few Days

Mrs. Wang Decided to Go with Him

Zeng Zhongming Did Not Go Due to Business

Gu Mengyu Went to Hangzhou Yesterday Afternoon

Central News Agency reported that the news that Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei was going to Europe for medical treatment was confirmed by many parties yesterday. President Wang decided to go abroad in three to five days, and Mrs. Wang Chen Bijun also decided to go with him. Zeng Zhongming was unable to go with him due to business. Wang is scheduled to return to China within the leave approved by the Central Government. The details are recorded as follows:

Gu and Zeng Arrived in Shanghai: Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu and Deputy Minister Zeng Zhongming arrived in Shanghai at about 8:00 am yesterday by night train from Beijing. After getting off the train, Zeng went directly to Wang's residence on Xipushi Road to rest, and then went out. Gu went to Wang's residence with his wife at about 10:00 am and met with Mrs. Wang Chen Bijun and had a long conversation. He left at about 11:00 am and hired a car to go to Hangzhou for sightseeing via the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway. Zeng went to Knoll Hospital in the afternoon to meet with Wang to discuss the issue of going abroad for medical treatment.

Zeng's Talk: A Central News Agency reporter met Zeng Zhongming at the North Station yesterday morning and had the following conversation: (Question) Is it true that President Wang will go to Europe for medical treatment? (Answer) President Wang is suffering from a serious illness and does intend to go to Europe for medical treatment, but it has not been completely determined at present. (Question) Will Mrs. Wang and Deputy Minister Zeng go with him? (Answer) It has not been decided yet. (Question) What is the purpose of Deputy Minister Zeng's visit? (Answer) I came here to meet with President Wang to discuss the issue of going abroad for medical treatment. (Question) When will Deputy Minister Zeng return to Beijing? (Answer) I am scheduled to return to Beijing by night train tomorrow (that is, today). After the conversation, Zeng hurried into the car and left. Later, a Central News Agency reporter visited Zeng at Wang's residence in the evening and asked about the results of the meeting with President Wang. According to Zeng, Wang decided to go to Europe for medical treatment within the three-month leave approved by the Central Government in order to seek complete recovery as soon as possible and to be able to recuperate quietly. Although the date of departure has not been determined, it is expected that it will be possible within three to five days, because the three-month leave is very short, and if it is delayed further, he may not be able to return to China on schedule. Which country to go to has not been decided yet. However, Mrs. Wang Chen Bijun has decided to accompany him to take care of him. I am unable to leave my post and go with him due to busy official duties. As for Wang's opinion on the investigation team's report, Zeng said that it is not yet time to make a public statement. The report that Wang will convene a meeting in Shanghai before his departure is just speculation. He may exchange opinions with important figures in Shanghai.

News from the Chu Residence: Yesterday, the wife of Executive Yuan Secretary-General Chu Minyi told a Central News Agency reporter that Wang's tropical disease has now recovered slightly, but he still needs to change places to recuperate. Therefore, Wang has decided to go abroad for medical treatment. Whether he will go to Germany and when he will leave has not been determined. Mrs. Wang Chen Bijun may go with him, because according to Dr. Knoll, he hopes that Mrs. Wang will go with him, which will be more convenient. Whether Railway Vice Minister Zeng Zhongming will go abroad with Wang has not been decided yet.

Wang Has Not Been Discharged from the Hospital: Yesterday, it was reported that Wang had been discharged from Knoll Hospital and returned to his private residence on Xipushi Road. According to a deep visit by reporters to Knoll Hospital, Wang was still recuperating in the hospital yesterday. The rumor that he had been discharged from the hospital and returned to his residence was completely inaccurate. According to a Knoll doctor who spoke to a Western newspaper reporter yesterday, Wang is still recuperating in the hospital.

Gu's Visit to Hangzhou: Yesterday afternoon, a Central News Agency reporter visited Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu at his residence.

Page 10

According to his family, Gu took his wife and son by car to Hangzhou via the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway in the morning to visit and inspect the construction of the road. Gu will visit Hangzhou for a few days before returning to Shanghai.

National Salvation Organizations Joint Association 116

Telegrams Overseas Chinese to Help the Righteous Army

The National Salvation Organizations Joint Association of the city, as the winter season is approaching, the green gauze tent has been removed, and the Northeast Volunteer Army has lost its reliance and is suffering from hunger and cold, telegraphed to overseas Chinese to provide assistance. The original telegram said, "Since the Northeast was lost, a year has passed in an instant. People are plotting against us, and they are getting an inch and a foot. The disasters are not only for the compatriots in the three provinces, but also for the people in the deep waters. Recently, the investigation team's report has been released. Looking at its suggestions, the sovereignty of China is in name only. It is known that the League of Nations attaches importance to power and ignores justice. If we want to survive, we must be self-reliant. To restore the lost territory and wash away our national shame, we only need iron and blood. Our Northeast Volunteer Army has risen one after another under the trampling of the strong enemy's iron hooves. Wherever the voice of righteousness is broadcast, the thieves and captives are defeated. Jinxi has repeatedly asked for help, and Shenyang has been besieged again. The reason why they have not been able to drive the enemy out of the country is that they have not received sufficient supplies. It is enough to know. When the green gauze tent is removed and the cover is completely lost, and the winter season is approaching, there is a lack of clothing and food. The northeast is bitterly cold, even in normal times, there is still a fear of freezing. The enemy's aid is increasing day by day, and a big battle is imminent. If there is not enough assistance, alas, my righteous army will not be defeated by the enemy's artillery fire and aircraft, and will also die from hunger and cold. Thinking of this, the heart is painful. The country has been suffering from disasters and famines for years, and the soldiers and bandits are suffering from them. The people are exhausted and poor, and they cannot afford to live. The government is sitting and misunderstanding the opportunity, and they are unable to make any progress. The people are talking emptily about saving the country, and they are only groaning. The wind and rain are drifting, and the boat is few. It is really the autumn of survival and death, and we have to cry out to our overseas compatriots. We hope that you will be passionate about protecting the motherland, and that you will be saddened by the disasters of the three provinces. We hope that you will rush to the aid of the needy and donate generously. In the future, when the Japanese prisoners are swept away and the skin work is achieved, it will be the strength of all of you, and the people of the whole country will have the glory to implement it. Urgent statement, I hope you will pay attention. Xiong Xiling, Chu Fucheng, Niu Chuanshan, Li Cishan, Wang Boshu, Liu Shixiong, Chen Dingyuan, Ni Guanghe, Wang Yiping, executive directors of the National Salvation Organizations Joint Association of the Republic of China, kowtow."

Northeast Volunteer Army Air Force Sends Personnel to Europe 117

Our people, in view of the crisis in the Northeast, are more aware that it is not enough to provide our Volunteer Army with sufficient material and spiritual supplies to boost their morale, recover the lost land, and return our rivers and mountains. Moreover, although the morale and momentum of our 19th Route Army in Shanghai to resist Japan was brave, it ultimately felt that it was difficult for a clever woman to cook without rice. When enemy planes came to attack, there was no way to stop them, and they were allowed to drop bombs, burn, and slaughter. This is what our people are most distressed about. At present, the people are automatically engaging in long-term anti-Japanese national salvation, so they plan to catch up quickly, collect money to purchase aircraft, and gather combat-trained talents. Once Guangxi flying coach Huang Yuanbo and Hunan pilot Li Binghui and other aircraft arrive in Shanghai, they will fly to the front to carry out national salvation work. In addition, Zhu Jiqing, the commander-in-chief of the Northeast Volunteer Army, directly appointed Xiao Buyun, the former director of Hunan Aviation and the anti-Japanese pilot of the 19th Route Army, as the commander of the Northeast Volunteer Army Air Force, and immediately sent him to Europe and North and South America to promote aviation to save the country to overseas Chinese, raise funds to purchase aircraft, save our Northeast, and recover the lost land. Xiao, whose name is Shaoshi, is from Xinhui. He is honest and generous. Six years ago, when he was interning in combat flying in the United States, he also served as the general manager of the Chinese Public Association in New York and other major ports. Therefore, overseas Chinese in the United States believe in his personality especially urgently. This time, the people's recommendation of Xiao to go to Europe and the United States to purchase aircraft and raise funds will be very effective. It is heard that the funds donated will be used entirely to expand the air force army for long-term national salvation.

News from the Righteous Army Ambulance Team Yesterday 118

Since the establishment of the Northeast Volunteer Army Ambulance Team, many patriotic youths from all over the country have come to the team to request to join. However, the team's goal is to provide ambulance, so those who do not have considerable medical and military knowledge will not be accepted. According to Jiang Huan, the deputy captain of the team, dozens of people have come to the team every day to request to join, which shows the general public sentiment. As for soliciting shares and contacting various business groups for supplies, the results are still good. However, the departure expenses are particularly difficult. Because of the days of soliciting donations from the outside world, the amount obtained is still small, which inevitably affects the departure date. However, within one or two weeks at the latest, the first batch of team members will definitely find a way to depart. The number of people is around 50, so that the wounded Righteous Army can get ambulance as soon as possible. They are currently rushing to complete the departure procedures. Also, the donations raised by the former Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of Secondary School Students amounted to nearly 10,000. In addition to assisting General Ma Zhanshan, there are still remaining funds, which are currently deposited in a bank in the city. Yesterday afternoon, the Secondary School Federation convened a meeting of various schools to discuss the disposal of the funds, and notified the Northeast Volunteer Army Ambulance Team to send personnel to report on the organizational significance and current situation, so that the funds could be allocated for assistance. The discussion resulted in a portion being directly remitted to the Northeast to assist the Northeast Volunteer Army, and a portion being allocated to the Righteous Army Ambulance Team for departure expenses. However, because the number of people who arrived yesterday was insufficient, it was not convenient to vote immediately. Another meeting will be convened this week to decide.

Residents' Representatives from the Designated Area of the New North Station Site Petition Again

Because the Ministry's Telegram Added Over a Thousand Mu of Land

The Pengpu Municipal Committee Promised to Forward It for Review

The Ministry of Railways, for the construction of the new North Station, has included the Pengpu and Zhenru districts within the railway construction zone. Because the designated area was excessive, residents from Wangjiajing, Zhangjiazai, Zhuxiang, and other places in the Pengpu district previously organized a petition group to appeal to the Ministry of Railways, requesting a reduction in the land requisitioned to alleviate the people's hardship. The Ministry of Railways replied that the currently designated land was not yet final and was subject to change in the future. However, recently, Railway Minister Gu Mengyu telegraphed Shanghai Mayor Wu, stating that for the new station, it was necessary to purchase additional land within a range of approximately 1,000 meters north of Jiaotong Road, west of Zhongshan Road, and about 680 meters long from east to west. This has affected the villages of Zhaojiazai and Lujiazai.

The residents in the vicinity are perplexed as to why the Ministry of Railways needs to include such a vast area. Therefore, over a hundred households from these two villages each sent a representative to form a petition group, which merged with the existing petition group from Wangjiajing and the other three villages, totaling over five hundred households. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, each household sent a representative, totaling over five hundred people, who first went to the Pengpu Municipal Committee Office to petition. Committee member Ling Zhibin personally received them. The representatives elected Zhao Chubei and Zhao Youting to speak, stating that the Ministry of Railways only needed 700 mu of land for railway construction, but the Railway Bureau had designated over 4,000 mu. Now, even 4,000 mu is not enough, and they are expanding it by another thousand mu. They are unsure what the Ministry's intention is. They have heard rumors that the Ministry intends to buy the designated area and then sell it at a high price, which may not be without reason. Therefore, they requested a prompt solution to alleviate their situation.

Committee member Ling replied that he would forward the petition to the municipal government for review. The petition representatives dispersed at 2:00 PM. It is also reported that the municipal committees of the four districts of Jiangwan, Yinhang, Zhenru, and Pengpu previously received orders from the municipal government to prohibit the sale of land within the area designated by the Ministry of Railways in the four districts, as the land prices needed to be determined after a three-week investigation. Now that February has arrived, far exceeding the three-week period, and the municipal government has not yet issued a decision, the four district committees intend to petition the municipal government to issue an order quickly. They are currently drafting the petition.

The Deng Zhongxing Store Was Attacked with a Bomb

Investigation Reveals Minimal Damage

The Deng Zhongxing Hardware Store at No. 736 Fujian Road, founded by Deng Jinchu from Guangdong, had recently received warning letters from the Red Blood Hoe Group. Yesterday evening at 8:00 PM, the store received another warning letter delivered by someone wearing a blue Zhongshan suit. The store staff opened the letter, and while they were passing it around, a bomb suddenly exploded outside the store's display window facing Guangdong Road. People in the store scrambled for safety, but because the bomb's force was weak, only a section of the glass was shattered, with no other damage. The store immediately reported the incident to the Lao Zha Gate police station, which dispatched a detective to investigate and took the bomb fragments and letter back to the police station for filing.

Xangzhai County Government Prohibits Private Occupation of Official Rivers

The Xiangzhai County Government has discovered that ignorant farmers have been filling and encroaching on official rivers since Yu Xinjun and Xin Junzhen. If this is not stopped promptly, it will inevitably lead to others following suit, which has a significant impact on water conservation. Yesterday, County Magistrate Yan issued instructions to all public security sub-bureau chiefs along the river to investigate at any time and issued a notice to the public along the river prohibiting arbitrary occupation of public rivers. Those who dare to deliberately violate the rules will be prosecuted.

Local News 2

Following Hu Hongji's Tragic Death

The Body Was Transported to Shanghai Yesterday

Temporarily Placed in the International Funeral Home

The Encoffining Ceremony Will Be Held on the 19th Before Returning to His Hometown for Burial

Hu Hongji, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, was traveling by car from Shanghai to Hangzhou on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway the day before yesterday afternoon when the car overturned near Haiyan Station, resulting in a tragic accident. Mr. Hu suffered severe injuries and died after some time. Details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday afternoon at 4:30 PM, Mayor Wu's wife and Municipal Secretary-General Yu Hongjun and others personally went to Mr. Hu's residence to offer condolences. Details are as follows:

The Body Was Transported to Shanghai

After hearing the news, Mrs. Hu, accompanied by Shen Hao, the head of the First Section of the Municipal Health Bureau, Wu Liguo, the head of the Second Section, and Sun Jiazhai, a medical technician from the bureau, traveled to Haiyan by three cars and one ambulance yesterday morning at 6:00 AM. They transported Mr. Hu's body to Shanghai by ambulance, arriving at the International Funeral Home at 4:30 PM in the afternoon, where it will be temporarily placed. The encoffining ceremony is scheduled for the 19th, after which the body will be transported back to his hometown in Wuxi for burial. A portrait of Hu Hongji is included.

Details of the Accident

Yesterday, a reporter from this newspaper went to Mr. Hu's residence to investigate the details of the accident. According to reports, at 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, Mr. Hu, accompanied by Mr. Gereke, the Director of Medical Education of the American Health Association, and several Chinese friends, traveled by car from the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway to Hangzhou for a visit. Mr. Hu and three Chinese friends were in one car, while Mr. Gereke and other Westerners were in another car in front. The car was originally driven by a chauffeur, but upon reaching Haiyan Station, Mr. Hu took over as the driver. Before driving two miles, the tragic accident occurred. It is said that in the car, in addition to Mr. Hu, who suffered severe injuries and died, only one person was slightly injured, and two were unharmed. It is reported that Mr. Hu was 40 years old and left behind five children, the eldest of whom is only 11 years old. His elder brother, Hu Songming, is engaged in commerce.

Many Visited to Offer Condolences

Yesterday, those who visited Mr. Hu's residence to offer condolences included Mr. and Mrs. Zhang Qun, Mayor Wu's wife, Huang Fu, Municipal Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Director of the Health Department Liu Ruiheng, and Director Jin Baoshan, who came to Shanghai from Nanjing specifically to offer condolences and assist in handling Mr. Hu's funeral and related matters.

Brief Biography of Mr. Hu

Hu Hongji was from Wuxi County, Jiangsu Province, and was 40 years old. In 1917, he graduated from the National Medical College of Peking. In 1924, he obtained a Doctor of Public Health degree from Johns Hopkins University in the United States. He served as the Deputy Director of the Shanghai-Songhu Commercial Port Health Bureau and has been the Director of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau for six years.

A telegram from Hangzhou on the 16th stated that after Hu Hongji died in Haiyan on the 15th, the Provincial Highway Bureau sent Inspector Ye Jichun to care for Hu's wife, Zhou Wenzhu, on the 16th. At 10:00 AM on the 16th, accompanied by Shen Hao and Wu Liguo, heads of the Shanghai Health Bureau, they transported the body back to Shanghai. According to Wu Chongren, the Magistrate of Haiyan County, Hu's motive for coming to Hangzhou was to test drive a car at the invitation of Mr. Huili, the owner of the Huili Automobile Company. Those who suffered the accident together were Zhang Zukang, the owner of the Shanghai Zhang Chongxin Sauce Garden, Wu Lusheng, a former employee of the Shanghai Finance Bureau, and the driver. Wu Lusheng's injuries were also serious and was sent to Hangzhou Guangji Hospital on the morning of the 16th. Zhang Zukang and the driver suffered minor injuries. Hu was driving the car at the time of the accident.

The Newspaper's President Will Come to Shanghai to Appeal

Organize a Petition Group to Achieve Its Goals

Issue a Declaration Requesting Assistance from All Sectors

The fresh pork industry in Jiangsu Province is protesting the business tax on pigs. The business tax bureaus in Jiangbei, Jingjiang, Rugao, and Taixing counties have been renting civilian houses in various ports since September 21st to collect business tax on pigs passing through, at a rate of two jiao per pig. Industries across Jiangsu Province have risen up in opposition, repeatedly sending telegrams of protest and sending representatives to Shanghai to jointly discuss countermeasures to ensure consistency. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, a special meeting of industry representatives from various counties was held in Nanshi. Over 60 representatives from various counties, including Cai Jinqing, Wang Shusheng, Chen Jinrong, Zhang Tongxing, and Wu Xishan, decided to organize a temporary joint association of fresh pork industry representatives from various counties in Jiangsu. 2. ) Representative Wang Shusheng proposed that if the petition is ineffective, an appeal be filed with the Control Yuan in accordance with the law. The proposal was adopted.

3. ) Representative Qi Wenyao proposed that our industry has been subjected to illegal oppression for a long time. Please organize a joint office of various industries as a permanent institution. The proposal was adopted.

4. ) Representative Cai Xiqing proposed that the taxes that have been coerced and illegally collected should be returned uniformly. The proposal was adopted.

5. ) Zhang Tongxing proposed that a lawsuit be filed in accordance with the law to punish the director of the tax bureau who illegally levied donations. The proposal was adopted.

6. ) Representative Gu Baoxiang proposed that the association should hire legal counsel. The proposal was adopted to hire lawyers Feng Xizui and Zhang Bingjun as legal counsel for the association.

7. ) How should the association's funds be raised? The decision was made that the representatives would donate the funds without raising additional funds.

Finally, it was resolved to issue a declaration requesting assistance from all sectors.

Xian Municipal Ferry Changes Schedules

The First Bus from Gaoqiao at 6:30 AM Every Morning

The opening hours of the ferry in this city have been reduced by one early and one late, as is customary from October 16th to March 15th of the following year. The first bus from Donggou to Shanghai and the first bus from Gaoqiao is actually the second bus. It is learned that the ferry general management office of the Public Utilities Bureau has recently increased the number of passengers in Gaoqiao, and the second bus arrived at the Copper Man Terminal at 8:50, which is too late. In order to meet the needs, starting from October 16th of this year, the first bus from Gaoqiao will be changed to 6:30 every morning. All other matters will be handled as usual. Therefore, if Gaoqiao passengers take the earliest bus, they can arrive in Shanghai at 7:50.

Local Supplement of the Shen Bao: Truth or Falsehood? Liang Zuoyou's Donation of Gold

Buddha: Any strange and bizarre event must have its indirect cause. Airplanes and wireless telegraphs can be called marvels. However, whether borrowing the power of electricity or the power of air, scientists are merely using them to make inventions.

Regarding the matter of Liang Zuoyou donating 30 million yuan, I initially suspected it, thinking that the "thousand" might be a mistake for "ten." Later, as the telegraphed news continued, I realized it was true. Now, the truth has turned into a question. What exactly is Liang Zuoyou selling in his gourd? We still don't know. However, Liang Zuoyou has been living in Beijing for a long time and couldn't even scrape together money for room and board. Such a rich man, indeed, I have not only never seen, but also never heard of. Is it the supernatural power of the monk Ji Dian, or is it Zhuge Liang's empty fort strategy played on the city wall?

There are many suspicious points about Liang Zuoyou donating 30 million yuan.

1. How could Liang Zuoyou, who possesses 70 to 80 million yuan in assets in a country with such backward production as ours, have a family name that has never been heard of?

2. How could Liang Zuoyou, who possesses 70 to 80 million yuan in assets, live so safely and without any losses in the bandit-ridden area of eastern Shandong?

3. Even if Liang Zuoyou has assets, how could he throw away 30 million yuan without any hesitation? Even generous overseas Chinese have not been heard of donating such a huge sum.

4. If Liang Zuoyou is such a generous person, why didn't he donate a single penny when Ma Zhanshan and the 19th Route Army were fighting against Japan?

Looking at the above points, Liang's donation of a huge sum is inherently suspicious. Now, it is becoming even stranger. Liang has been living in Beijing for a long time and hasn't even handed over a single penny. Even his room and board are guaranteed by the ministry. Simply put, not a single penny can be explained. Who has ever seen a rich man who doesn't have a single penny to his name? But since he doesn't have a single penny, how dare he make such grand pronouncements and petition in Beijing? That is the first suspicious point. Liang not only promised to donate a huge sum, but also researched the usage of the funds quite thoroughly. As the saying goes, "acting as if it's a big deal." That is the second suspicious point. Therefore, saying it's true seems definitely not true. Saying it's false seems not false either. A ten-foot-tall monk leaves one completely baffled.

Someone said that Liang Zuoyou's donation of 30 million yuan is a strategy. In reality, Liang only donated one silver dollar. His idea is that if the 30 million people of Shandong province each donated one yuan like Liang, then 30 million yuan could be obtained. If they each donated two yuan, then 60 million yuan could be obtained. If that's the case, it's truly making a fool of the world. Why doesn't Liang say he'll donate 400 million yuan? Our country has 400 million people. If each person donates one silver dollar, then 400 million yuan can be obtained. If each person donates two silver dollars, then 800 million yuan can be obtained. This kind of wishful thinking is not only in Liang Zuoyou's mind. Everyone has probably had such wishful thinking.

Therefore, no matter what, I cannot believe Liang Zuoyou's donation of 30 million yuan.

Uneven Development

Bo Xiong Takes Responsibility, Receives Salary

Scientific Electric Eye and Its Uses

Zuo Qi

What is called an "electric eye" is an electrical device that is unusually sensitive to light. It is a recent invention, so not many people know about it. However, in the past year, photosensors have made rapid progress. The uses of electric eyes are becoming more frequent, with discoveries almost every day. They have great uses in industry and in methods of daily life. From cinemas to factories, from arenas to traffic lights, from laboratories to kitchens, electric eyes are needed everywhere. Electric eyes can be divided into four categories, each with its own special properties and uses: (1) Phototube or photocell: This is a vacuum or gas-filled cell containing a photosensitive metal plate that emits electrons when exposed to light. The emitted electron flow is then amplified using another vacuum tube. (2) Selenium cell: Selenium is an element with a photosensitive property: its resistance is extremely high in the dark, and almost no current flows through it. However, under strong light, it becomes a good conductor, and a lot of current flows through it. The amount of electricity it conducts is directly proportional to the brightness, that is, the size of its resistance is inversely proportional to the brightness. Sealing selenium in a vacuum tube creates a selenium cell. (3) Photovoltaic cell: This type of cell can generate current changes with changes in light intensity. (4) Vaporized metal plate (such as vaporized copper, etc.): It can generate a relatively large low-voltage current when exposed to light.

Wherever a beam of light can be interrupted, changed, or controlled by some method, the various photosensitive cells mentioned above can be used to perform calculations, detection, or capture, without hindering the object or action being calculated, detected, or captured in any way. For example, to have a standard clock's pendulum drive other clocks without adding weight to itself, just use a beam of light and a photocell to accurately record the back-and-forth movement of the standard clock pendulum without hindering its operation at all.

In television (i.e., wireless transmission of images), the photocell is an important tool. Its function is to convert changes in the brightness of an object's surface into changes in electric current so that they can be transmitted to distant places.

Photocells installed at the entrances and exits of tunnels can count the number of cars traveling through the tunnel. A special meter is installed in the manager's office of a movie theater, allowing them to know at any time how many viewers are in the theater.

In the future, an important use of electric eyes will be to adjust the brightness of indoor lighting. Just as we currently use thermostats to automatically adjust the indoor temperature, we will use a "light regulator" to adjust the intensity of lighting in factories or schools.

The use of photoelectric devices as security devices has already had significant results. For example, punching machine workers can use a beam of light and a photocell for protection. When their hand enters a dangerous area, the light beam is immediately interrupted, cutting off the motor's current and stopping the punching machine abruptly. Several large department stores in the United States have installed photocell safety switches on elevators. When someone enters a beam of light shining in the elevator's path, the elevator operator cannot close the door or start the machine, thus avoiding the occurrence of danger. Automatic door openers can be installed on private carports using photocells. When the car is ready to enter the carport, the driver only needs to point the car's headlights at the electric eye hidden at the entrance of the carport, and the door will open with a creak.

Since electric eyes have so many uses in industry and daily life, if we do a little more research, we can also use them in hospitals to provide various conveniences for patients. For example, hospitals have large doors that must be opened frequently, but patients do not have the strength to open them themselves. With photoelectric devices, the door will open automatically with a simple gesture from the patient. Similarly, a simple action such as raising a hand or shaking the head can also be used to ring a bell to call or send a signal to a waiter outside the room. When it gets dark outside, the indoor lights can be made to turn on automatically. And when the morning light arrives, the windows can close automatically so that patients can comfortably enjoy their breakfast in a warm room. There are many other wonderful uses that are too numerous to mention.

In short, the greatest feature of the electric eye is the flexibility of its arrangement. Whenever and wherever a shadow or light can be used to control a task, this ever-vigilant electric eye can always tirelessly fulfill its duty.

Suggestions from the Society for Improving Society on the Adoption of Common Form Characters

Chi Fo

As human affairs become more complex, the function of writing becomes greater. If one engages in meticulous word-chopping, imitating the writing styles of the Qin and Han dynasties, the Six Dynasties, or the Tongcheng School, not only is there no time for such leisure, but it is also insufficient for practical application. Therefore, the writings of Sima Qian and Ban Gu, parallel prose, and classical prose can only be left to literary masters for research. For the sake of practical application, we naturally need to use vernacular Chinese. As for the characters themselves, no one has paid attention to them yet. I, however, advocate the adoption of common form characters. Although they do not conform to the principles of the six categories of Chinese characters, elementary philology, and the Shuowen Jiezi, that doesn't matter because all that matters is convenience in application.

Originally, writing is a symbol of thought. Now that human affairs are so complex, as long as there are symbols, why bother talking about "elegance" and "vulgarity"? For example, "yuan" in "foreign yuan" (foreign currency) should originally be written as 圓 because the character is complicated, it has been changed to 元! 圓 is also written as 园. Removing the enclosure becomes 元! There are many common form characters. When old-fashioned scholars see them, they will definitely say they are nonsensical. In fact, many common form characters are very ancient. For example, the common form character 祘 is the ancient character for 算 (calculation). The ancient character for 燈 (lamp) is 鐙, and the common form is written as 灯, with very few strokes. There is no question of vulgarity.

The transformation from seal script and greater seal script to clerical script and regular script, and from clerical script and regular script to running script and cursive script, is simply because human affairs have become more complex, and time has become more precious, so changes are needed to create a form of writing that is easy to write. Common form characters are the same. Following the natural course, they will naturally change. If one says that common form characters cannot be written because writing them is too vulgar, then please do not write running script or cursive script. Just carefully write seal script and clerical script. Thinking about it carefully, one might smile wryly at the silliness.

In short, the benefits of adopting common form characters are great: (1) They are easy to write, and (2) they save time. In this era of complex human affairs, there is indeed a need to promote them. Just look at how the invention of shorthand has had a great effect. Writing is originally a symbol of thought. The words "elegant" and "vulgar" are not an issue. I very much hope that the Ministry of Education will adopt my humble suggestion and ask experts to compile a "Dictionary of Common Form Characters." If there are friends who study elementary philology, I also hope that they will compile a specialized dictionary to preserve the essence of our country. Our country's writing is made very meaningfully. For example, the character 男 (man) is composed of 力 (strength) and 田 (field), indicating that men should engage in agriculture and not just pursue "officialdom and wealth." It also proves that our country is founded on agriculture. Adding 勇 (brave) above the character 男 (man) creates the character 勇 (brave), so those without courage are not considered men. Also, for example, the character 勞 (labor), with two 火 (fire) characters above, indicates that a rise in liver fire is the main cause of consumption. This is also very consistent with hygienic principles. I have briefly mentioned a few to give a glimpse.

A Corner of Society, a Wrongful Death at Sea

Shi Ben

"[You * * *, will you confess? If you don't, I'll make you suffer!]" The young mistress of the Zhang family, sitting in the position of a judge in the bedroom, secretly interrogated A Hong, the maidservant who was the subject of this secret case discovered last night. Kneeling below, A Hong lowered her head, her eyes full of tears, her body trembling incessantly. At this moment, her heart was uneasy, fully revealing her frightened and flustered state, worried that her secret dealings had been discovered by the young mistress and that she would definitely receive a severe punishment. Although this matter was entirely done under the threat of the young master, how could she explain it to the young mistress? In her mind, waves of thoughts surged like this, so she didn't answer a word to the young mistress's questions, only sobbing and shedding tears.

"Huh! You're doing well, still not confessing. Do you think you can cry your way out of this? Hmph, hmph, I suppose you won't confess without being tortured." Mrs. Zhang, in a fit of anger, stepped down from her seat and grabbed a two-foot-long bamboo stick from the corner, ran up, and randomly struck A Hong's back several times with a cracking sound, while shouting, "Will you confess? Will you confess? Are you going to confess?"

"Oh! Mistress, save me! Alas, alas, alas..." A Hong could only cry and scream.

"Still not confessing, I see you still have a hard mouth." Seeing that A Hong still hadn't confessed, the young mistress rolled up her sleeves, picked up the bamboo stick, and gave A Hong a second beating on her mouth, striking A Hong so hard that her mouth was full of blood.

"Ah yo! Mistress, don't hit me anymore! I'll talk, alas, alas, alas..."

"Okay, you talk. If you talk, I'll forgive you."

"Ah yo! How can you ask me to talk?" A Hong, forced by the young mistress, couldn't bear it any longer and thought she had to confess directly to avoid punishment. But then she thought that it would be shameful to say it, so she was in a dilemma, wanting to speak but stopping.

"Hurry up and say it. Exactly how many times have you slept with the young master, and how much have you cheated him out of? How did you * * * last night? Tell me everything properly, and I'll forgive you. Otherwise, your life will be in danger."

A Hong was still young and timid, and when she heard that her life would be in danger, she was frightened out of her wits, her face ashen, covered in sweat, and immediately confessed: "Mistress! Once."

"Nonsense!"

"Really, only once. Only once last night."

"Is that so?" "Never mind whether it's once or twice. I'm asking you how you seduced the young master." The young mistress's face was filled with the color of jealousy, and her eyes immediately became sharp, darting left and right, as if she was waiting for A Hong's satisfactory reply.

"Mistress, I'm innocent! I never seduced the young master. Last night, the young master came to my room himself."

"You're good at sweet talk. Not only are you shameless yourself, but you also say that people are forcing you. Hmph, how could a young master like ours be interested in a stinking thing like you? Quickly tell me the truth, or I'll hit you again."

"Mistress, really, last night, the mistress went out to see a movie. I was in my room, doing my work, and the young master barged in, without asking why, he pinned me down on the bed. I struggled desperately and tried to shout. Mistress, this is all the truth. If the mistress says it's not true, then beat me, and even if you beat me to death, I won't say anything else."

"Hm! Get up. I'll call your mother here tomorrow, and we'll talk then." At this point, the case was clear, and the female judge retired from the court, busy handling the procedures for sentencing.

The next day, A Hong's mother came, and the young mistress said to her, "Your daughter is misbehaving here, specializing in stealing things. I discovered it yesterday, so I called you here today to take her back." So A Hong's mother took her back home, constantly complaining to her: "Little girl, you really don't know how to behave. It was so good living in the Zhang family. Who asked you to be unruly and break this golden rice bowl? I'll see you starve to death when we get back."

Alas, poor A Hong. "Swallowing coptis chinensis while mute," she had no way to explain. She died bearing the false charge of "misbehaving and stealing things." The humiliating tragedy of being raped by the young master has been wrongfully buried at sea.

Random Thoughts, Casual Notes

Fearless

Does celebrating National Day mean the country will perish from now on? Or will China become strong from now on? If these words were true, then I would be willing not to celebrate for the rest of my life, but I think things are not that simple. The gentlemen who proposed this matter are too far-sighted, I think. We Shanghainese have a saying, "A green-bellied monkey," which means someone who doesn't remember things. But I think the two Lius and others probably also know that the people hate civil war, but they still bravely point their guns inward. Although many people have advised them, they still want to do it. Their unwavering spirit makes me admire them, but at the same time, our saying can be used to prove this. Poor our noble country, it's like Wang Xiaoer celebrating the New Year, each year is worse than the last. I remember that the year before last, on National Day, there was still a lantern festival, with very enthusiastic celebrations. Last year was still okay, but this year, it's pitiful to say, it's become silent and odorless. If we continue to have civil war, non-resistance, and no revitalization, I'm afraid we'll have to fly the flag at half-mast this time next year.

Short Story, Modern Absurd Drama

Onlooker

"Adulterous Couple"

Characters:

Mr. Jiang Ren: A bored gigolo (30 years old)

Tian Woman: A licentious and promiscuous woman (45 years old)

Mr. Zhu: A foolish man (50 years old)

Setting:

The bedroom of an ordinary family, with various photos of beautiful women hanging on the walls!

Scene 1

(Mr. and Mrs. Zhu are making a big scene, the man kneeling before his wife, the wife holding a ruler, threatening to hit him.)

Zhu: I didn't mean to break the rice bowl. They told me to stop, I didn't stop them!

Tian: I toil all day long to feed you, you good-for-nothing!

Zhu: But, but your every action, I never interfere!

Tian: Dare you? Dare you? I'll do whatever I want, it's none of your business. As long as I'm happy, I can do whatever I want.

Zhu: But... but... this time, you must forgive me. Let me get up and walk! (Trembling)

Scene 2

(The two are sitting side by side on the bed, acting coyly.)

Tian: Darling, look how easily I can suppress men, especially useless ones like this!

Jiang: You're really something! A real woman of valor!

Tian: But we have to find a way to get him to another place. Having him around is really annoying.

Jiang: I think we should have him be a teacher again. Luckily, the principal of ×× School is an old acquaintance of yours. He'll definitely be accommodating.

Tian: Dare you mention my past scandals? Is he my only old flame? If you talk nonsense again, how about I make you an old flame too?

Jiang: Haha! I... I... I'm deeper and further than a lover. I'm yours! ...... (While they are talking and laughing, they suddenly hear Mr. Zhu coming upstairs.)

Scene 3

(The three are sitting in the room, their facial expressions serious.)

Tian: (To the man) Do you know Mr. Jiang? He is my maternal uncle's brother-in-law's cousin, so we are distant relatives.

Zhu: I'm sorry, I don't know him. So, you're a respected relative, right? Sorry, sorry.

Tian: He doesn't need you to address him as "respected"!

Jiang: Mr. Zhu's intentions are good. Don't turn good words into bad ones. To be honest, you can be content to have a husband like him!

Tian: Why be content? Why?

Jiang: I... I... I won't tell you ......

Zhu: I want to go teach in another place again. Can you help me? Brother Jiang, please help me out.

Jiang: Of course, of course. We must find a way to get you settled in another place.

Scene 4

(After dinner at a certain hotel.)

Tian: Why were you so muddleheaded and talking nonsense in front of that turtle?

Jiang: What's the big deal? Even if he knows everything about us, what can he say? "If you want to do it, don't be afraid; if you're afraid, don't do it."

Tian: Really?

Jiang: Of course!

Tian ......

Jiang ......

(Curtain falls)

Market News

Vocational Education Society

In addition to the academic lectures and national crisis lectures that the China Vocational Education Society has already established, it is now adding education lectures in response to requests from various parties, specifically for colleagues of the society, school education staff, and people serving the community to conduct amateur studies. The lectures are tentatively scheduled for 6:00 PM to 9:00 PM every Saturday and 8:00 AM to 10:00 AM every Sunday. Lecturers are hired from experts in various fields. For the first period, starting in November, Mr. Shen Xinqing has been hired to lecture on the general idea of national studies and philology, and Dr. Chen Xuanji to lecture on educational psychology. Students will only be charged two yuan per semester to limit enrollment. Anyone wishing to join the lectures can register with the society at 80 Hua Long Road to request a copy of the regulations.

The Establishment of the Puyi Industrial Chemistry Research Society

Mr. Shen Jiao, a chemical industry expert and contributor to the science column of this supplement, recently pointed out that China's industrial chemistry is lagging behind and urgently needs to be promoted. However, the lack of industrial chemistry talent is a recognized problem, which has caused domestic factories to shut down due to a lack of talent or hire foreign technicians, resulting in a loss of sovereignty, which is extremely heartbreaking. Therefore, he has initiated the establishment of the Puyi Industrial Chemistry Research Society, using practical factory methods to guide students and conduct research on chemical industrial products for all sectors. All chemical products can be entrusted to the society for research. The society has accepted many research projects, and all have achieved satisfactory results. Those wishing to conduct research can contact the society at 55 Ximenli, Ximen Road, and a brochure is available for mail or in-person request.

Recent News of the 19th Route Righteous and Brave Army Alumni Association 121

The 19th Route Army Camp Student Volunteer Army Alumni Association held its eighth executive committee meeting at 9:00 AM on the 16th, on the third floor of the Zhenda Silk and Satin Store on Fourth Road. Twelve executive members attended, with Wang Pingnan chairing and Tu Shanyuan recording. The resolutions of the meeting are summarized as follows: (1) Regarding the issue of the association's application to establish a ten-man volunteer army training unit, the Shanghai-Woosung Garrison Headquarters forwarded an instruction from the Ministry of Military Affairs stating that it conflicted with the conscription law currently under review by the central government. The resolution was to temporarily suspend the application as instructed and proceed with the plan when the time is right. (2) Regarding whether the date of the regular meeting should be changed, the resolution was to abolish the fixed date for regular meetings. In the future, if there are important matters, the chief executive will convene meetings as needed. (3) Regarding the unanimous promotion of national salvation through aviation and publicizing the great lessons learned by our comrades during the January 28th Incident due to enemy aircraft in combat, the resolution was to notify all students to actively promote this. (4) Regarding the association's financial situation, from preparation to the present, approximately 150 yuan has been spent. The resolution was to request the chief executive to raise funds independently and not solicit donations from the outside. It is reported that the association has printed and distributed notices regarding the above matters to all students for their information.
